 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : The RCN Editor Staff                                          บ
 บ    Subject : Introduction : RCN Goes Biweekly                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Welcome to Reality Check Network, your #1 Warez E-mag!  And so we'd   บ
 บ  like to stay!  To meet further reader demand, the staff has decided that  บ
 บ  RCN will now be released on a biweekly schedule.  There won't be any      บ
 บ  less material found in each issue, the material will just be of even      บ
 บ  higher quality!  RCN will be released every other Sunday.  We believe     บ
 บ  that by giving ourselves more time between the release of each issue, we  บ
 บ  will be able to release a better RCN, and at the same time, the extra     บ
 บ  time will help create a more positive and less hectic work environment    บ
 บ  for the RCN Staff.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Again, you can always find Reality Check Network available on the     บ
 บ  WWW at HTTP://WWW.RCN.ORG/INDEX.HTML, as well as find some of our         บ
 บ  previous competition (though, unfortunately, none exists at the moment)   บ
 บ  and perhaps compare and contrast.  And as a final note, a little word     บ
 บ  about etiquette, purposefully placed at the END of the introduction.  I   บ
 บ  don't mind if you don't want to read an entire article or interview, and  บ
 บ  decide you've had enough in the middle, but if you're going to contact    บ
 บ  us with a complaint, make sure you HAVE read the entire text before       บ
 บ  doing so.  It doesn't look too impressive when you complain about         บ
 บ  something and our response to your complaint was in the body of the text  บ
 บ  all the while, but you were too lazy to find it.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As always, thanks for reading RCN, and don't hesitate to contact us!  บ
 บ  You can either join channel #RCN on the EFNet IRC network, or email us    บ
 บ  at an385786@anon.penet.fi.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It happened on the 17th of July when I was in a bad mood and took     บ
 บ  over channel #CD because I was auto-opped there.  So I massdeoped and     บ
 บ  kick those lamerz out.  I ignored all CTCP and then MSG's also.  In       บ
 บ  about 30 minutes I get killed by MikeySoft.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *** You were killed by MikeySoft (irc2.uiuc.edu!*.texas.net               บ
 บ      [ircd.texas.net] !*.kern.com [jnl@204.212.36.8]                       บ
 บ      !phx-ip2-131.getnet.com! MikeySoft (TakeOver/Flooding Retard))        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      With that kill, they get the channel back.  By the way, what rights   บ
 บ  has an IRCop to kill you for takeovers?!  I mean, there isn't such thing  บ
 บ  as OWNING CHANNELS!  They shouldn't have opped me in the first place.  I  บ
 บ  come back all pissed (I was on mo.net all the time) and messaged          บ
 บ  Incarnate bitching at him telling him that he is a lamer and that he      บ
 บ  needs a kill to take my ass down.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Then he said he used what he could so I told him that next time I     บ
 บ  will flood Mikeysoft off before taking over.  This cost me another        บ
 บ  fucking kill!!!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *** ERROR Closing Link: Twiztah[N/A@wn-brn18.sat.net] irc2.uiuc.edu       บ

 บ  noticed them releasing Bermuda Syndrome.  I had heard it was a really     บ
 บ  good game, even though it was big, so I tried it, and I definitely don't  บ
 บ  remember it being in Russian as Reflux claims.  FBI was a group           บ
 บ  dedicated to putting out good releases, not untranslated or non-working   บ
 บ  ones.  That was a great program, and I got much joy from letting others   บ
 บ  try it out, to see if they want to buy it, since I still feel that's the  บ
 บ  only right thing to do.  Remember, if everyone got the stuff for free,    บ
 บ  there wouldn't be any more of it!                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  out that Reflux duped the release, but to make it worse, they were        บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      You're going to be shocked when you read this reply.  Don't take it   บ
 บ  personally, it is not directed at you.  It's just a small bit about       บ
 บ  women that complain about their position in society and female rights.    บ
 บ  Rebel Chicken and I thought of this when we were at Safeway one day.      บ
 บ  I've been wanting to publish it for a while now, and it has absolutely    บ
 บ  nothing to do with warez, but it's something I've got to say and get      บ
 บ  e-mail back about, so people, don't hold back, I want to start a riot     บ
 บ  here, write me and tell me what you think of my little schpiel here.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Once upon a time Rebel Chicken and I walked into a Safeway (it's a    บ
 บ  supermarket in the USA) to get something to eat while on an RCN break.    บ
 บ  We walked past the magazines, they were on the way to the cashier, when   บ
 บ  Rebel Chicken stopped and exclaimed "HUBBA HUBBA!!!"  I turned around     บ
 บ  and saw him checking out this babe on the front of some magazine.         บ
 บ  "Ehhhhhhh ---- heeeeeeeeeellllo!!"  I shouted back.  So we were checking  บ
 บ  out the women on the front of magazines and then Rebel Chicken noticed    บ
 บ  something (just when you thought he was actually looking at the women).   บ
 บ  He asked me "Did you notice how every magazine cover with a woman         บ
 บ  pictured on it has something about sex?"  Surely enough, he was right.    บ
 บ  We looked through about 25 magazines, and found only two that didn't.     บ
 บ  One issue of "Seventeen" and the other I don't remember.  Sorry guys, we  บ
 บ  didn't look at computer magazines.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So this is the conclusion I draw from all this.  Women have no right  บ
 บ  in hell to complain about being treated like sex toys.  I'll tell you     บ
 บ  right now, I definitely would NOT have minded treating those women as     บ
 บ  sex toys heheheh but there's no way they can try to tell me that they're  บ
 บ  just showing off beauty with no sexual connotation implied.  Before       บ
 บ  women can complain about being treated like objects and having a lower    บ
 บ  place in society, they need to think twice about their actions.  I don't  บ
 บ  mind the fact that beautiful women pose for magazines, but when every     บ
 บ  magazine with them says something like "20 tips to make your sex life     บ
 บ  better," "A quiz to see if you really know your way around your bed,"     บ
 บ  "5 women reveal the SEXXXIEST summer lingerie," "The moves the men        บ
 บ  really like," or "Sex tips for the new year, happy 1996!" it degrades     บ
 บ  the women's level in society.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Right about now all the women's rights groups are telling me "I see   บ
 บ  nothing wrong with women doing this.  It shows that they feel more        บ
 บ  comfortable with issues about sex."  But so what?  Maybe the men don't.   บ
 บ  I don't know, I've never sexually molested a woman, and don't             บ
 บ  particularly plan on it, but others have, and I don't doubt that          บ
 บ  magazine covers such as the ones I'm speaking of had some part in it.     บ

 บ  he's got the smallest knowledge : size of brain ratio I've ever seen.     บ

 บ  something so revealing?  When you invite people to a party, you can't     บ
 บ  expect to kick them out when they show up at your door, and when you      บ
 บ  invite trouble, you can't expect to kick its hand off your ass.           บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Wassup Everyone!  This is just a little something I'd like to say     บ
 บ  about the interview done on AOD (Angel of Death) about LGN (Legion) and   บ
 บ  how they kicked out AcidPlain.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Everything that AOD had said was true.  I was in the group for about  บ
 บ  two days.  If many of you don't remember, I was the one who constructed   บ
 บ  the group's first diz.  I was approached by a senior (I think he was at   บ
 บ  the time) of the group, Samuraion.  He said that if I did a .DIZ for the  บ
 บ  group, I'd become a member and have access to all their sites.  I wasn't  บ
 บ  all that excited, but it would have been a good chance to get my art      บ
 บ  skills up to par.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So I went to another window, loaded up my ansi editor, and began to   บ
 บ  work on the diz.  Five minutes had passed and I had finished the diz.  I  บ
 บ  sent it over to Samuraion and he told me he liked it.  He gave me access  บ
 บ  to their channel, and told me that I would be added to the INFO as a      บ
 บ  member, and that I would soon have access to their site(s).  I was a      บ
 บ  little excited, thinking that this group would have a lot of success,     บ
 บ  and that I was a part of it (after all, without a diz, they wouldn't get  บ
 บ  far).  So I was given access, and soon became friends with a few people   บ
 บ  in the channel.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      All was going good.  I was couriering their releases as soon as they  บ
 บ  were being released.  I was doing the job that their couriers should      บ
 บ  have been doing.  I was grabbing their releases off a member's shell      บ
 บ  account, and sending them all around my a/c, and to other sites which I   บ
 บ  wish to keep anonymous.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I went into the channel a couple of days after the last release, and  บ
 บ  soon noticed after 5 minutes that I still had not been opped.  So I       บ
 บ  waited figuring I was lagged.  I waited, and waited, but still no +o.     บ
 บ  So I msged Acidplain, and he said he would go check the nfo file to see   บ
 บ  if I was in the group.  Turns out I wasn't in the latest nfo file, so he  บ
 บ  had no proof.  I told him that I was the one who did the DIZ for them,    บ
 บ  but still no ops.  I waited for Samuraion to come into the channel.  He   บ
 บ  came in about an hour after I first joined.  I told him that my ops had   บ
 บ  been taken away and that I was not in the NFO file.  He told me he added  บ
 บ  me, and said that he would do it again.  He sent me a copy of the latest  บ
 บ  one which had my name in it, and I kept it on my HD.  I joined the        บ
 บ  channel the next day, and to my surprise (yeah right), I was not given    บ
 บ  the ops.  I was added to the bot, and then got my ops back.  I was        บ
 บ  disconnected due to my computer freezing, and then connected back to IRC  บ
 บ  30 minsutes after.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I joined the channel again, and once again, no ops.  I was mad at     บ
 บ  this time, and so I sent a public message out stating that someone was    บ
 บ  removing my name out of the BOTS' list and that that was the reason for   บ
 บ  me not having my ops.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Samuraion joined the channel again, and he told me that he would      บ
 บ  once again add me to the bot.  I waited, and then had ops again.  I was   บ
 บ  then -o'ed and was wondering why.  I messaged Acidplain, and he said he   บ
 บ  didn't need me any longer because they had received a new diz and didn't  บ
 บ  want mine anymore.  I was fucking pissed (excuse the language).  So I     บ
 บ  left the channel, and msged X-Factor, and told him that Acidplain was     บ
 บ  asshole, and explained why I had called him that.  I got no reply, but    บ
 บ  when I joined channel #Legion, I was kicked out of the channel by none    บ
 บ  other than Acidplain.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I figured that whatever information I was giving to other members of  บ
 บ  the group, was being leaked out to Acidplain, so I said "Fuck This" and   บ
 บ  left the channel, never to return again.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So to all wondering if that interview contained some false            บ
 บ  information, none did whatsoever, whatever was said about Acidplain is    บ
 บ  true.  And I regret ever doing any work for that guy.  All respects go    บ
 บ  out to Samuraion for giving me a chance, and to X-Factor for being there  บ
 บ  when I needed help!                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Storm Hacker              บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I was on my favorite warez channel, #Warez66, and I had been asking   บ
 บ  around for some time now and no one seemed to be responding.  Then after  บ
 บ  time of waiting, to my joy, a guy named NetFrack goes "I do."  I quickly  บ
 บ  messaged him back, and he DCC's me this huge "Mywarez.nfo."  I shell to   บ
 บ  DOS to see what this nfo file is all about and, find out its a nicely     บ
 บ  arranged list of all this guy has!                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Overjoyed, I try to strike a deal with him, and ask him questions     บ
 บ  which indulges us in a conversation.  The thing that really surprizes     บ
 บ  me, is when I learned that he started warez only 8 months ago!  The       บ
 บ  biggest shock comes to me when he tells me he got his first computer in   บ
 บ  November of 1995!  His first experience with a computer he says was when  บ
 บ  he was 8 years old (a Comodore 64, at a Kids Centre) playing games and    บ
 บ  crap.  From then on, he dreamed of getting one.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Finally, after another 7 years his fascination with computers was at  บ
 บ  its peak, he bought one.  Though not knowing much about them, he decided  บ
 บ  to make the leap and finally managed to get Ma and Pa to get him one.     บ
 บ  Low on money he had to choose the most economical, a Pentium 75, with 8   บ
 บ  megs of ram.  After that, like any newbie, he went and signed up with     บ
 บ  AOL, Compuserve, etc.  He tried them all out.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      However, he was still not into the wonderfull world of warez until a  บ
 บ  friend of his gives him a copy of Doom 2, with group nfos and all.  He    บ
 บ  sees them and realizes that something very interesting out there exists,  บ
 บ  which he must find out about.  In December of 1995, he gets a real        บ
 บ  Internet account, and manages to figure out IRC in about 2 weeks.  From   บ
 บ  that time until now, he has managed to gather 2.2 gigs of warez (don't    บ
 บ  ask me how, he doensn't know either) and has even managed to join some    บ
 บ  groups, as an artist and a courier.                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This guy went from being a computer illiterate, to a warez god in     บ
 บ  such a short time.  What I'm trying to say is, if NetFrack can do it,     บ
 บ  all you newbies, pirates or not, can too!  All it requires, is            บ
 บ  dedication, and the willingness to go out and learn about the scene       บ
 บ  first!  Then the warez will come to you...                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Acid                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I was reading RCN #23 when I came to an editorial done by a member    บ
 บ  of RCN (HBKid).  It was regarding how release groups release programs     บ
 บ  which nobody would use, and how it's not their fault.  Here's a piece of  บ
 บ  his work :                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  "I guess it is not the release group's fault if the programmers these     บ
 บ  days are not making quality programs... have some pride and don't         บ
 บ  release 'How To Type Faster Part 5' when they know people don't use it."  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      When I read this, I thought to myself "But it is the release group's  บ
 บ  fault."  The fault is not at the programmer.  People do use these         บ
 บ  programs <as lame as that may seem>.  They are used in school, in         บ
 บ  training programs, etc.  There are many programs out there which may      บ
 บ  seem dumb, but in the professional world, and not in this fantasy world   บ
 บ  we live in, the programs are very important, and are used by thousands    บ
 บ  of people through out the world.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This is just a word of advice to the release groups.  Even though it  บ
 บ  is a VERY hard job these days to find and release a good game or util,    บ
 บ  you must also stop and think that not everyone in the scene will give     บ
 บ  you the credit for it (as HBKid said in his article).  There are many     บ
 บ  people in the scene who will take advantage of the release, and use it    บ
 บ  for their personal use, but the majority will only look at the release,   บ
 บ  and go onto the next.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *PS* "Quality Over Quantity!"                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Storm Hacker              บ

 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This is a letter in reply to 'Da Phreak's' letter in RCN #22.  I      บ
 บ  really feel he should look harder into what he is talking about.  He      บ
 บ  asks :                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      "I mean, who is the thief here?  Us or them?  They charge $50 for a   บ
 บ  piece of plastic and some magnetic tape, and I AM THE CRIMINAL for        บ
 บ  getting it for free?"                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Yes, my friend, you ARE the criminal.  Obviously he doesn't know how  บ
 บ  hard coding can be.  I'm sure he's unaware that it took iD YEARS to make  บ
 บ  quake the game it is and they should be rewarded.  This is why Mr. Law    บ
 บ  Making Guys have tried to protect these programmers from people like us.  บ
 บ  Later on, Da Phreak states:                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      "I mean, there is a chance <1 in 1 000 000 000> that I could          บ
 บ  randomly write binary that would replicate this last scene from a well    บ
 บ  known 3D game."                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Once again, his ignorance shines through!  Let's look at some very    บ
 บ  elementary probability:                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      (Let's assume 'this last scene from a well known 3D game' is 200k):   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      200x1024=204800 bytes                                                 บ
 บ      204800x8=1638400 bits                                                 บ
 บ      2^1638400= REALLY BIG.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So you see, it's a bit bigger than 1 : 1 000 000 000.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now before someone calls me a hypocrite for saying all this, I'd      บ
 บ  just like to say that I accept how much work programmers put into their   บ
 บ  games.  I accept I'm a ciminal.  I just don't care. :-)                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Mr. Phallus               บ

 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This letter is partly in response to Ermac's letter in RCN #21 about  บ
 บ  the benefits and popularity of IRC Couriering, and partly my opinions     บ
 บ  and other feelings about IRC Couriering.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      IRC couriering, in my opinion at least, may show which files are the  บ
 บ  more popular ones, but with BBS trading (I don't do FTP trading), I know  บ
 บ  that you can find more online about the file you are going to download,   บ
 บ  as well as have a more reliable and faster connection to get the file     บ
 บ  from.  Often, when leeching off a DCC bot on IRC, you have to wait for a  บ
 บ  slot to become available, and when that does, how are you to know the     บ
 บ  bot won't drop connection while sending you the file.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I know that when I BBS trade I can upload or download simulateously   บ
 บ  while knowing that I can get a connection on most multinode boards        บ
 บ  whenever I want, and know that the board is stable and won't disconnect   บ
 บ  in the middle of my transfer.  With IRC couriering also, you may be       บ
 บ  getting decent rates thru a t1 or t3 on your provider from the bot, but   บ
 บ  then, after it reaches your hd, you have to sit and wait while            บ
 บ  downloading it off your providers drive.  Now, this can be hasslesome,    บ
 บ  and I do know that many will go through this trouble just to get an 0     บ
 บ  day release, but it's not THAT beneficial timewise.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now, I don't want to sound like guys who setup DCC bots on IRC are    บ
 บ  lame, or stupid, I think that those who have bots steady going 24/7       บ
 บ  offering the latest files in any offer channel are very taleneted and     บ
 บ  should be commended.  I personally think though, that IRC Courering       บ
 บ  leaves the trading scene too simple.  I enjoy trading locally, and on     บ
 บ  occasional 800/888s, and I only use DCCs to get mags and small files      บ
 บ  (under 200k).  I enjoy the competition that trading gets on boards        บ
 บ  trying to beat other guys who have the same files.  IRC trading gievs     บ
 บ  people the "no ratio" advantage of taking files off IRC returning         บ
 บ  nothing, and then becoming well known.  I hope to start telnet trading    บ
 บ  soon, but right now I'm rebuilding my board from a hard drive crash, and  บ
 บ  don't have much time on my hands between that and work, so BBS trading    บ
 บ  is all I can do.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Finally, I'd like to address Ermac's saying that groups like          บ
 บ  Everlast and RiSC should get dcc channels and offer bots.  I personally   บ
 บ  would like to commend Everlast and RiSC and all other groups that only    บ
 บ  trade where the REAL competition is, on boards and sites.  Anyone can     บ
 บ  sit on IRC for a few hours a day offering some new files they DCCed from  บ
 บ  someone else, but it takes                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      someone who is fairly talented to trade the fast files on the         บ
 บ  fastest boards and sites in the world.  Again, I don't think all DCC      บ
 บ  guys are bad, fATE did a good thing creating #fATEfiles, but it got way   บ
 บ  to popular and blown out of proprtion.  I have a lot of friends in fATE   บ
 บ  or who used to be in fATE, and have respect for the group itself.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In my area, I'm glad to see trading picking up because of IRC, but    บ
 บ  many people ask me why I don't just move my board to real fast, and       บ
 บ  leech off IRC all day.  The reason is, it's too easy.  Again, no          บ
 บ  competition and no ratios.  That's why sites and boards gain the          บ
 บ  importance they do.  Most TRUE traders get the files off the whq's or     บ
 บ  group affiliated sites, and spread from there.  IRC trading has been      บ
 บ  given too much importance in the scene.  IRC should be left as group      บ
 บ  channels to have group information publicly available, and in some        บ
 บ  cases, just a meeting place between fellow members to talk.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  King Cobra                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear RCN,                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      How hard is it to find a god release these days?  That is a good      บ
 บ  question when you really think about it.  When BBSing and trading files   บ
 บ  how many files that you download do you actually use?  When looking at    บ
 บ  files these days they seem really pathetic.  For instance, why would      บ
 บ  someone want a personal heatlth manger or something that is very boring.  บ
 บ  3D Creative caladers and other lame releases I have seen passed around    บ
 บ  and when checking my BBS stats it seems that these files are never        บ
 บ  downloaded while Duke Nukem 3D on my board was downloaded 75 times!!!     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I think that release groups should take more time and release         บ
 บ  quality things that a majority of people would like instead of wasting    บ
 บ  time cracking and passing around total junk.  For instance, I must have   บ
 บ  traded and seen over 5-7 gigs of files and how many of those files did I  บ
 บ  actually use?  Hardly any to be perfectly honest, in my time in the       บ
 บ  scene I might have used about 500 megs of all the things releases and a   บ
 บ  lot of the things that I used were the older files which I had to         บ
 บ  request because most of the newer things out there aren`t even that       บ
 บ  great to begin with.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I guess it is not the release group's fault if the prgrammers these   บ
 บ  days are not making quality programs to crack but I do think they should  บ
 บ  have some pride and don't release "How to Type Faster Part 5" when they   บ
 บ  know people won't use it.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The problem these days is people are just couriering for fun... for   บ
 บ  something to do and they will trade almost everything and not even use    บ
 บ  it so release groups can get away with releasing junk because they know   บ
 บ  people will trade it no matter what it is.  So release groups that read   บ
 บ  this letter and think about the quality of your releases lately and ohh   บ
 บ  yea try to make sure they work to.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Couriers read this and remember next time you courier "How to Cook"   บ
 บ  maybe if you refused to trade some lame releases like that maybe the      บ
 บ  groups will stop releasing them!                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  HBKid                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Introduction : AMN vs. RISC                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Since before I can remember when, courier groups have been battling   บ
 บ  over which courier group was #1 in this and that, blah blah.  Courier     บ
 บ  Group A would steal a good courier from Group B, and then Group B would   บ
 บ  get mad and then Group B would steal a good courier from Group A, and so  บ
 บ  on.  Courier groups would steal a member here, and a member there for     บ
 บ  the sake of improving a group's couriering ability.  However, with the    บ
 บ  advent of the Internet, and the structuring of the few but well           บ
 บ  organized FTP sites, many courier groups are now switching their          บ
 บ  attention into battling over FTP sites instead.  A good FTP courier       บ
 บ  could be found anywhere, but a good FTP site is hard to come by, and is   บ
 บ  heavily sought after by group leaders.  Group leaders risk (no pun        บ
 บ  intended) a few back stabbings here, and lie a bit there, and do          บ
 บ  something lame somewhere else, just for the chance that they might be     บ
 บ  able to acquire a few of these important FTP sites.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The following is a story of how RISC steals (I could use a more       บ
 บ  passive word, but what the hell for?) a FTP site from Amnesia.  Amnesia   บ
 บ  is caught with its pants down, and the owner of the FTP site, Ryu, who    บ
 บ  happens to be an Amnesia member, is stuck in a Catch 22 scenario.  A      บ
 บ  long, long, time ago (last week), in a galaxy far away (Oregon), an       บ
 บ  Amnesia siteop is ganged up on by his friendly (back stabbing) RISC       บ
 บ  cositeops, and thus, loses control... here goes...                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Abo-bo> Do you know about Ryu and Oasis and the situation between        บ
 บ           Amnesia and RISC?  Do you know the situation there?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Pand> No, I do not, but just tell me the information and I will see to   บ
 บ         it that the higher ups at RCN will get this information.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Abo-bo> Well, here is the situation, Ryu and Vile started a site named   บ
 บ           The Doughnut Hole with Ryu and Vile as siteops.  We'll refer to  บ
 บ           that site as the The Doughnut Hole for sake of anonymity.        บ
 บ           Later on, Vile dropped out of the site for a few weeks, and Ryu  บ
 บ           asked Devast to help out as a cositeop.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Pand> Please continue...                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Abo-bo> Then, the site became the Prestige USHQ and the Amnesia Courier  บ
 บ           HQ.  At this point, Devast lied to Ryu to try to get him to      บ
 บ           drop Amnesia and go with RISC.  Ryu told Devast and RISC that    บ
 บ           he did not want to drop Amnesia for RISC (refer to the           บ
 บ           interview with Ryu in RCN #23).  At that time, Devast kept on    บ
 บ           trying to get The Doughnut Hole to go with RISC by getting Ryu   บ
 บ           to drop Amnesia.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Pand> I see, is there anything else?                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Abo-bo> Ryu repeatedly slammed Devast's ideas to go with RISC.  Ryu's    บ
 บ           logic was that Devast wanted RISC only for his own personal      บ
 บ           gain by schmoozing the higher ups of RISC.  And Ryu did not      บ
 บ           want that kind of shit to happen on his site.  The fact of the   บ
 บ           matter was this, Devast thought that he owned the site now.  No  บ
 บ           matter how much work he thinks that he put into the site, Ryu    บ
 บ           was still the one housing the hardware.  If the feds had         บ
 บ           knocked down the door, Ryu would go to jail, not Devast.  This   บ
 บ           was and is Ryu's site.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Pand> So the actual site is like in Ryu's room?                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Abo-bo> After this, the hardware needed to be moved to another location  บ
 บ           for reasons that I am not willing to reveal.  An unnamed person  บ
 บ           volunteered to house the hardware under the stipulation that it  บ
 บ           whould still be Ryu's site.  The only difference would be that   บ
 บ           the hardware was in a new local.  The day after the unnamed      บ
 บ           siteop gave that promise to Ryu, he took that back after Ryu     บ
 บ           had decided to boot Devast from the site.  Ryu wanted Devast     บ
 บ           out because Devast was using the site for personal gain and for  บ
 บ           selfish motivations.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Pand> Yuck...                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Abo-bo> At this point in time, the siteops and cositeops decided that    บ
 บ           they wanted to drop Amnesia again, and bring in RISC.  It's      บ
 บ           funny since 4 of the 7 siteops and cositeops are RISC members.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Pand> Whoa, I guess RISC secured that site.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Abo-bo> Ryu would not let this happen.  He stated before that his site   บ
 บ           would not go to RISC, and now, by Devast's undermining, the      บ
 บ           site was again trying to do so!  Ryu stated the fact that he     บ
 บ           would leave the site as a siteop if they booted Amnesia, which   บ
 บ           they did.  So Ryu is no longer a siteop on The Doughnut Hole.    บ
 บ           I have a log that I took with Devast, Revolver, and myself.  I   บ
 บ           want this published so that the scene knows what a whining,      บ
 บ           sniveling, and backstabbing little bitch that Devast really is.  บ
 บ           Can I dcc you the log file?                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Pand> Go right ahead, I would really appreciate it.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Ryu Loses His Site                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The following is a log file which details how Devast justifies        บ
 บ  ousting Ryu from The Doughnut Hole.  Devast claims that he was the one    บ
 บ  who started the site and that he is the sole reason why the site was a    บ
 บ  success.  However, the truth is anything but what Devast claims it to     บ
 บ  be.                                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      For those of you who are currently leaders in a courier group, or     บ
 บ  would someday like to be running a group, it would be good to either      บ
 บ  learn how to be sly like Devast, or to learn how to outsly someone like   บ
 บ  Devast.  Either way, Devast has a lot to teach us.  You can either learn  บ
 บ  to be like Devast, and catch other people with their pants down, or you   บ
 บ  can learn how to prevent from being fucked over by people like Devast,    บ
 บ  and thus, prevent getting yourself caught with your pants down.  Read on  บ
 บ  and decide for yourself.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Session Start : Thu Aug 01 02:05:53 1996                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Devast> Ryu has been removed from The Doughnut Hole staff.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Revolver> What the fuck for!?!                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Devast> The Doughnut Hole is now the Razor WHQ.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Revolver> What the fuck for!?!                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Devast> I didn't want to remove him from the staff.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Revolver> I want to know all the decisions that have been made since     บ
 บ             the phone call with Ryu.  I want to know every detail, and     บ
 บ             this will be logged.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Devast> Ryu said, "If the site drops Amnesia, I am gone."                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Revolver> Why has the site dropped Amnesia?                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Devast> We had a vote on whether or not to drop Amnesia and Ryu's vote   บ
 บ           was accounted for as a "no."  The deal to boot Amnesia off the   บ
 บ           site was made by 5 people who were on the weektop.  They only    บ
 บ           had 2 that wanted to keep the site Amnesia.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Revolver> You are sooo damn stuck on getting rid of Amnesia!  Why is     บ
 บ             that so??                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Devast> Amnesia does nothing for the site.  Amnesia only leeches.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Revolver> I don't understand why you literally hate Amnesia.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Devast> I don't hate them.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Revolver> Amnesia has 4 damn traders in the top uploaders.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Devast> I just don't think that The Doughnut Hole should be an Amnesia   บ
 บ           site.  There was a staff vote and people voted 5 to 1 in favor   บ
 บ           of dropping Amnesia.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Revolver> Who is on staff besides Coolio, Ryu, and yourself?             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Devast> Arch-Vile, Cyberjack, and Darkside are all part of the staff.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Revolver> These guys are obviously biased against Amnesia because they   บ
 บ             are all in RISC!  Which fucking group do you think they will   บ
 บ             vote for?  It's all rigged man and you know it.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Devast> So what?  The vote was to drop Amnesia and Ryu was part of the   บ
 บ           vote, but lost.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Revolver> Who started the fucking site??                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Devast> I did.                                                           บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Aslan                บ
 บ    Subject  : A Retired Legend          Affiliation : ex-Malice VP         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: While in the scene, what groups have you been a part of?  And what  บ
 บ        were your positions in those groups?                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ASL: Well let me see, when I was calling a UK board called the flying    บ
 บ        teapot (using a different handle at that time) I guess I was not    บ
 บ        in any groups.  This is because I guess one could class me as       บ
 บ        inept in the warez of the scene, but I contributed whatever I       บ
 บ        could to the board.  In 1992, I joined a small Internet group       บ
 บ        called FC.  Although one could not class it as a serious group in   บ
 บ        terms of trading, warez, or speed, I still feel that FC held the    บ
 บ        foundations of what the scene, the true scene is all about.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What foundations did this group hold which makes up the true        บ
 บ        scene?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ASL: The true scene is not just phreaking, carding, but the fact that    บ
 บ        you share friendships which in my opinion is a thing that should    บ
 บ        happen now.  As well, one can see the bullshit in groups is         บ
 บ        growing nowadays, group fights, etc.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What happened after you joined FC, when did you take leave for      บ
 บ        other courier groups?                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ASL: After FC, where I met the likes of Stingray 6 and Cruger of RISC    บ
 บ        (Rise in Superior Couriering), I joined RTS (Request to Send),      บ
 บ        under the leadership of Dorian Hawkmoon and Ordnance.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What were your duties in RTS, and what did you accomplish while in  บ
 บ        RTS?                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ASL: Reflecting back on RTS, my main job was to coordinate their         บ
 บ        Internet side, and I thought I was doing good job, however          บ
 บ        problems with the leadership made me leave RTS along with Dorian    บ
 บ        Hawkmoon and a few others to form the group Malice.  With Vile and  บ
 บ        Dorian's assistance, we rebuilt Malice with Jake the Snake.  At     บ
 บ        first, I was a member of Council, but as more pressing duties       บ
 บ        arose, I was given the position of Vice President.  Given the       บ
 บ        charge of Malice was an honour to be bestowed on me, and I knew I   บ
 บ        wanted to run Malice a little differently from most groups out      บ
 บ        their.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How did you want to run Malice differetly?  What did you have in    บ
 บ        mind that would have made Malice stand out above the rest?          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ASL: I tried to inspire good teamwork and a friendship enterprise        บ
 บ        within the group which I say must have worked because Malice back   บ
 บ        in its haydays was damn friendly and the members were easy going.   บ
 บ        By having a good karma within the group, I felt this would give     บ
 บ        Malice the edge over the rest.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How was Malice dominant while you were leading it at its peak?      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ASL: Well, Malice did have problems with other couriering groups out     บ
 บ        there, but times have now changed.  While leading Malice along      บ
 บ        with Jake the Snake, Dorian, Lester, and company, everything went   บ
 บ        like clockwork.  Malice conquered Europe and certainly the UK,      บ
 บ        where there was no other competition.  So while Malice was          บ
 บ        expanding, I sought to make the group afilliated with more utils    บ
 บ        groups and gain strategic alliances with games groups.  Thus, I     บ
 บ        joined smaller utils groups like Darius and Pinnacle, and games     บ
 บ        groups such as Razor 1911 to ensure that Malice could and did       บ
 บ        spread the warez.  By having a small voice in this and that group   บ
 บ        and by establishing good team work between the releasing groups     บ
 บ        and Malice, I envisaged that the Malice future should have been     บ
 บ        bright.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Should... but something unfortunate did happen to Malice.  What     บ
 บ        turned your friendly Malice members into bitter Malice members?     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ASL: However, since the problems with Malice in the last two months,     บ
 บ        which may I add has been rectified by the current leaders, I have   บ
 บ        left all posts because I was getting tired of it and I wanted to    บ
 บ        finish my degree and do a Ph.D.  What happened to Malice with       บ
 บ        Amnesia and Rapier is public knowledge so I do not wish to follow   บ
 บ        that on.  Currently, since I am retired from all this, the only     บ
 บ        thing I occasionally do is act as the independent siteop on         บ
 บ        Enigma.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Do you have plans to ever come back to Malice once you have         บ
 บ        finished your Ph.D.?                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ASL: Well, that would be in 3 years time haha, I really can't say.  I    บ
 บ        do give some advice where needed, but I am tired of it all, and     บ
 บ        warez just doesn't interest me anymore.  Sure, the boards still     บ
 บ        retain some interest in the UK, where I like talking to the         บ
 บ        sysops, but otherwise, I find the act of downloading warez via      บ
 บ        molyturbo to be boring and basically unintresting.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Which field is your doctoral degree in?                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ASL: My Ph.D. thesis will cover the development and the application of   บ
 บ        the Information Superhighway for the benefit of the people with     บ
 บ        special needs.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: I have a special need for warez.  You can interview me for your     บ
 บ        doctoral thesis.  And I can go grab Darkhosis, he'll be your net    บ
 บ        monkey, and you can give him tests, and you can give me warez.      บ
 บ        Anyhow, what does Aslan stand for?  What does that word mean?       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ASL: Haha, Aslan... well, if you're Turkish, Aslan would mean "lion."    บ
 บ        However, if you read C.S. Lewis' books, Aslan is the good lion who  บ
 บ        defends Narnia from the White Witch.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What do you think of the current state of the couriering scene?     บ
 บ        Do you think much has changed since you were an active leader of    บ
 บ        Malice?                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ASL: The current state, well, that's a good question, if you split the   บ
 บ        couriering scene between boards and the Internet, it is obvious     บ
 บ        the attention is shitfing away from boards and toward the Internet  บ
 บ        for the sake that it it is easier to courier to and it's faster.    บ
 บ        The only group that I can think of that is like moffo dedicated to  บ
 บ        the boards is Everlast, possibly RISC on their HQs and once upon a  บ
 บ        time Malice on all their boards throughout the world.  But the      บ
 บ        emphasis appears to be on the Internet, so there seems to be a      บ
 บ        whole load of new Internet groups that appear week by week but I    บ
 บ        am probably mistaken.  This would also imply that the Internet      บ
 บ        scene appears to be reaching a saturation point as you can only     บ
 บ        have so many Internet groups out there.  As for when I ran Malice,  บ
 บ        I ensure that (tried to anyway) that my region, the UK, got its     บ
 บ        boards covered well and that our sites in Europe got covered.       บ
 บ        Also, before RISC took over Enigma and before Malice had its        บ
 บ        difficulties, Malice did support Enigma damn well.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: So, if the scene is saturated, does that mean that it is GOOD or    บ
 บ        BAD for the scene?                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ASL: Well, maybe a new blood will bring new attitudes, proving to        บ
 บ        people that they don't have any ego problems and that they have an  บ
 บ        idea what teamwork is all about.  I think the scene could do with   บ
 บ        more of those types of people be it boards or the Internet.  Some   บ
 บ        people take the scene far too seriously and think you have to be    บ
 บ        elite and shit, and if you aren't elite, you have to be lame.  All  บ
 บ        I can say is, the scene embraces those who believe in the right     บ
 บ        ideology.  That's why when one of your writers, Trite, criticized   บ
 บ        Malice, I wrote a letter based on facts and sound arguments, not    บ
 บ        hysterical rantings and ravings that some people can give.  So      บ
 บ        yeah, new people with decent ideas might not be a bad idea.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Mind you Trite is no longer a part of RCN, and is no longer         บ
 บ        allowed to submit articles to RCN.  :)                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ASL: Well Trite I think has improved certainly, but as I say, never      บ
 บ        judge a person by his or her cover until you know them.  As some    บ
 บ        people say, there is an alpha and there is an omega.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: And a Win 95 Beta... is there anything you would like to say to     บ
 บ        the scene before we adjourn?                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ ASL: Let us all try and make what we have left in the scene a better     บ
 บ        place be it on the Internet or on a board.  Because if we don't,    บ
 บ        then we will be the final destructors of a hobby in which we all    บ
 บ        participate and enjoy.  Remember, it's only a hobby guys and        บ
 บ        girls.  Oh yeah, hi Steve, Duncan, Robert, Gary, Andreas, Philip,   บ
 บ        Marten, Tom, Justin, and everyone who knows me.  :)                 บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Holy Beast           บ
 บ    Subject  : Prestige Senior Cracker   Affiliation : Prestige Cracking    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How long have you been in the scene?  Once you became a part of     บ
 บ        the scene, how long was it before you started contributing to       บ
 บ        various groups, and how did you contribute to each of these         บ
 บ        groups?                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PSG: I've been in the scene for about 7 years now.  I started with       บ
 บ        coding demos for demo groups, and some of those were Apocalypse,    บ
 บ        Neurotica, and Rebels.  This was back in 1991, after that, I left   บ
 บ        the demo scene and started coding viruses and some antiviruses,     บ
 บ        but I soon got bored and started cracking for the IBM/PC, I         บ
 บ        cracked/coded for Scotch which merged with PWA and then I left PWA  บ
 บ        to join Hybrid in 1993.  After that, I joined FairLight where I     บ
 บ        was cracking/organizing together with JBM.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Wasn't FairLight a group that specialized in releasing floppy       บ
 บ        games?  What happened after the floppy games scene died out?        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PSG: Well, when the floppy games scene died out, I carried on to groups  บ
 บ        like TDT, Mortality and finally Prestige and Siege which I am in    บ
 บ        now.  Oh, I was also in Dynamix, but what the hell...               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Because you have been in the scene for such a long period of time,  บ
 บ        and because you've been active in various groups while being in     บ
 บ        the scene, you can be considered a good witness as to the scene     บ
 บ        happenings throughout your time.  In your expert opinion, what is   บ
 บ        happening to the scene now, how has the scene changed in the past,  บ
 บ        and how do you feel it will change in the future?                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PSG: I've noticed that the competition is less now in the IBM/PC scene   บ
 บ        and loyality is becoming a thing of the past.  More and more        บ
 บ        people are more interested in their own success and they don't      บ
 บ        care about the groups they are a part of.  I think that the IBM/PC  บ
 บ        game scene is going to die out in the future because the games are  บ
 บ        getting bigger and bigger, and there aren't many good crackers      บ
 บ        around that can do the job.  It won't be worth ripping the games    บ
 บ        in the future.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Even if games get bigger in size, isn't it also logical to assume   บ
 บ        that transfer speeds between end downloaders will also increase at  บ
 บ        the same rate?  According to Krypto's indepth study on download     บ
 บ        times, which can be found in RCN #23, Krypto concluded that it      บ
 บ        took the average downloader 2 hours and 19 minutes to download the  บ
 บ        average 2 meg game in 1988 at 2400 b/s, and that it also takes the  บ
 บ        average downloader 2 hours and 19 minutes to download the average   บ
 บ        28 meg game in 1996 at 33.6 kb/s.  If that is true, then the size   บ
 บ        of the game is not going to effect the scene because transfer       บ
 บ        speeds will be going up as well.  How long do you think the IBM/PC  บ
 บ        scene will survive?                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PSG: The scene will never die out totally, but it will be totally        บ
 บ        different and as we already can see the quality isn't going to be   บ
 บ        the most important goal.  I think the scene will survive 6-7 more   บ
 บ        years and then die out.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: When you speak that, "quality isn't going to be the most important  บ
 บ        goal," are you referring to games groups that are indifferent to    บ
 บ        quality?  If so, do you believe that there are games groups out     บ
 บ        there which do stand for quality?                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PSG: Honestly?  I believe that there are no groups at the moment which   บ
 บ        are releasing 100% quality.  They are all so anxious to get the     บ
 บ        games out.  It's not like in the C64 time when the group that       บ
 บ        released the best cracks and trainers would win the release.  And   บ
 บ        I can understand how the groups feel since what you are releasing   บ
 บ        can never be 100% quality since you are ripping out a lot of        บ
 บ        stuff.  The games scene right now is doing a very good job          บ
 บ        advertising for game companies.  We release a ripped "demo" for     บ
 บ        the game so that everyone can test the game and if they really      บ
 บ        like it, they have to buy it to get everything.  It wasn't like     บ
 บ        that back in the floppy days, since you would get the *WHOLE*       บ
 บ        game.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Even in the floppy days, you could use the same reasoning and say   บ
 บ        that you never downloaded a *WHOLE* game because you never got to   บ
 บ        download the manual.  Then, in order to get the *WHOLE* game, you   บ
 บ        had to go out to buy the complete game at some software store.      บ
 บ        Anyhow, why is the IBM/PC scene so different from the long ago C64  บ
 บ        days?                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PSG: One of the reasons might be that people who bought a C64/AMIGA,     บ
 บ        bought it to *PLAY* on it.  It was all about games.  On the         บ
 บ        IBM/PC, 30 to 40% of the games have protection, if you can call it  บ
 บ        that.  Back in the C64 scene, the crackers were often the leaders   บ
 บ        of groups and they were doing most of the job.  They had the whole  บ
 บ        game.  Most IBM/PC crackers today don't receive the whole game,     บ
 บ        and when you know you're cutting on the quality when ripping the    บ
 บ        game, you don't really feel like making trainers, docs and nice     บ
 บ        intros for it.  And most importantly, the scene is split into 2     บ
 บ        scenes, a demo scene and a cracking scene.  Before, those two were  บ
 บ        the same and the cracking groups released quality demos too.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How did these two scenes which were originally one, split off into  บ
 บ        two?                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PSG: Since the values changed, a good release isn't a release with a     บ
 บ        nice intro.  Intros, demos, and maybe nice trainers became less     บ
 บ        important to the cracking scene.  So leaders soon stopped asking    บ
 บ        for intros because that was no longer an important issue for the    บ
 บ        leaders who wanted game releases.  The demo people understood the   บ
 บ        situation and left the cracking scene and started their own scene.  บ
 บ        And there is such a big difference between the demo scene and the   บ
 บ        cracking scene because you don't work a lot on one game/release.    บ
 บ        But a good demo might take over a year of work!                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
