 บ    Reporter : Celestian                 Interviewee : Pussy                บ
 บ    Subject  : Fucking the Scene         Affiliation : n/a                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Hello, I've heard some things that I was wondering if you could     บ
 บ        confirm for me?  I've heard that you've been framing other people   บ
 บ        and taking down warez sites.  Is this true?                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PUS: Yes, quite exciting stuff!                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Why are you doing this?                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PUS: It's fun, VERY FUN!                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: It's Fun?  You're sitting in channels #Freewarezdcc and #Warez666,  บ
 บ        snagging what you can I'm sure, so why are you hurting the scene?   บ
 บ        Why don't you try helping the scene?                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PUS: Because that's not fun.  It's fun to see them squirm as I delete    บ
 บ        all their files after downloading them for my personal use.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Are you a cop?                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PUS: No.  Cops usually leave the evidence for the FBI in the big         บ
 บ        situations.  Cops don't delete sites.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Uh huh... how is it that you can bypass security which would keep   บ
 บ        you from deleting files?                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PUS: :)                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Ok, well, I'll be publishing this in this weeks issue of RCN #24,   บ
 บ        is there anything you would like to say to the scene in general?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PUS: Yes, there actually is.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Please do...                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PUS: I just want everyone to know that the warez community will not be   บ
 บ        a success until the warez community stops.  Software publishers     บ
 บ        spend quite a while on the programming and creation of their        บ
 บ        software, and I fully back them.  If I like a title, I buy it.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Ok, we all encourage people to buy the software if they like it.    บ
 บ        Let me ask you this, how many sites have you taken out?  And do     บ
 บ        you know the names of the groups in which you've hurt?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PUS: I think it's upwards close to a thousand sites.  It's kinda hard    บ
 บ        to keep track of.  I especially like to delete quite a few of them  บ
 บ        NVC (New Vision Couriers) sites.  They are VERY LAME!               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What about big name courier groups?  Have any luck with those?      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PUS: Actually, I did get a couple FATE (Fast Action Trade Exchange)      บ
 บ        sites.  I think I ended up getting kicked off after I got about     บ
 บ        half of the files on them.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: I see.  You said up above that the warez community needs to stop,   บ
 บ        and that if you like a certain title you go buy it.  However, you   บ
 บ        just made a contradiction in terms.  You are in the warez scene to  บ
 บ        review software to see if you like it before you buy it.  Why       บ
 บ        don't you just get out of the warez scene and buy the software      บ
 บ        that sparks your interest?                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PUS: Well, demo versions usually really suck, so warez is nice to do a   บ
 บ        quick play with, then delete.  But most people have huge warez      บ
 บ        collections and never buy the full versions.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: I see, but in a sense, you do the same thing as everyone else, so   บ
 บ        you too are supporting the scene.  Without it, you wouldn't know    บ
 บ        what to buy and what not to buy either.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PUS: I enjoy watching the idiots search for programs, it's funny as      บ
 บ        hell.  I don't care about them, I don't care if it lasts.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, it looks like we have yet another asshole on our hands.  This   บ
 บ  one seems to be even more destructive than our old pal Chris Carter.      บ
 บ  This guy is IP spoofing our very own IPs with a program which he wrote    บ
 บ  himself.  I tried to get it from him, but he wouldn't release it.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      After he looks like you by spoofing you, he jumps into the channel    บ
 บ  that you were in and then somehow gets the addresses to the groups        บ
 บ  sites.  He gets on the sites, takes what he wants, then somehow breaks    บ
 บ  security and deletes everything on the site.  He can be found on the      บ
 บ  Undernet under the handle PuSsy, however, from what I understand, he      บ
 บ  likes to impersonate others a lot, so watch out!  This was the address    บ
 บ  that I got on him at the time of speaking to him.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      PuSsy is jgearon@pmx1z01.kcnet.com * Josh Gearon                      บ
 บ      PuSsy is now on #nowarez4u #freewarez #freewarezdcc                   บ
 บ      PuSsy using Chicago-1.IL.US.Undernet.org [199.0.154.14] American      บ
 บ      Informations Systems-Chicago                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      One day, as I was checking my site lists, I came across a deleted     บ
 บ  site and then another and another.  It's not an uncommon thing for one    บ
 บ  but three in a row!  I noticed that they were all being deleted by the    บ
 บ  same person, the dreaded "Pussy."  People have speculated about whether   บ
 บ  warez is legal, and the answer is plain and simple NO.  But that's what   บ
 บ  makes warez all more fun.  Why would someone go and delete what is a      บ
 บ  passtime for millions of traders and "jobs" for crackers and coders?  Is  บ
 บ  it fun for them to torment us?  No one will know unless they know the     บ
 บ  few deleters out there.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I frequent a few warez channels and the occasional #WarezX channels,  บ
 บ  and all you hear is "That damn Pussy got site #2," or "That fucking       บ
 บ  Pussy, I hate his ass, he deleted the site I was on."  Or even the        บ
 บ  occasional playing of the Rip 96 file_id.diz.  I know I have said those   บ
 บ  things too, but is it really that bad?  Are these "lamers" really         บ
 บ  hurting us?  Is it causing the scene to fall apart?  The answer is NO to  บ
 บ  all three questions. Yes, I said NO.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Many don't realize it but they are helping us.  They are forcing      บ
 บ  more of us to find private sites and forcing curriers to find             บ
 บ  delete-restricted sites.  These things are not bad and infact they help   บ
 บ  the scene.  Private sites force non-eleetists to groups, which help the   บ
 บ  scene of course, and delete restricted sites force hackers to find        บ
 บ  better sites or work on their hacking skills so they can get root, and    บ
 บ  while doing that improving their skills.  Private sites are better and    บ
 บ  faster and delete-restricted sites help better group hackers.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      All-in-all, they are nothing more than a pro for the scene rather     บ
 บ  than a con.  Although it is annoying when they delete while your on a     บ
 บ  site, but most people carry more than one list with them.  I would like   บ
 บ  to say I do not encourage deleting, but bashing them will make it worse.  บ
 บ  Just let them be and they will quit.  If not, work around them and join   บ
 บ  a group.                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Hades                     บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Rancid Apathy        บ
 บ    Subject  : Coredump Senior           Affiliation : Coredump's Success?  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Coredump is relatively new to the scene, yet it has proven in the   บ
 บ        last few weeks that it can dish out games as well as the other      บ
 บ        more established games groups.  What has been the driving force     บ
 บ        behind Coredump's success?                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CD: Well, we are trying to bring some quality back into the scene, and  บ
 บ        stay professional about it too.  We have to remember that the       บ
 บ        scene is for fun, and we're all in it together.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How has Coredump been able to bring back quality to the scene?      บ
 บ        What makes Coredump stronger than other games groups, if that is    บ
 บ        the case?                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CD: As a new group, we are trying to stay as organized as possible.     บ
 บ        We strive to release working, non duped and properly cracked        บ
 บ        games, by testing them and making sure they are ready.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Has it always been Coredump's policy to make sure that all          บ
 บ        Coredump releases are properly cracked?  Also, on the note of non   บ
 บ        duped games, could you mention a few Coredump releases that would   บ
 บ        be categorized as non duped and quality?                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CD: We are a new group, as you noted, and have had small problems in    บ
 บ        the past, but our policy is to make sure that the games are ready   บ
 บ        to play after installation, 100 percent.  I would categorize Quake  บ
 บ        as a quality release from Coredump.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Coredump has made some mistakes in the past, and I would not        บ
 บ        consider them as small, but nonetheless, it's a thing of the past,  บ
 บ        and Coredump has most definitely improved upon itself.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CD: A new group is bound to make mistakes, and we can use those         บ
 บ        mistakes as something that we will not let happen again.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: On the note of Quake, wasn't that already released by 2 other       บ
 บ        games groups before Coredump released its version?  Could           บ
 บ        Coredump's version of Quake be a dupe?                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CD: ROR supposedly released Quake Final, but it wasn't even the final.  บ
 บ        ROR's release of Quake can't be put in the same category as         บ
 บ        Coredump's release.  We're not talking about a FINAL Beta release   บ
 บ        of a game here.  Razor 1911 also released Quake, but it was         บ
 บ        released after Coredump had already released its version.  Our      บ
 บ        version was out before theirs.  Razor had a quality release, and a  บ
 บ        good job to them.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: A good job to Razor?  That's a good attitude to have, however, I    บ
 บ        don't think Razor is repaying your nice compliment with a nice      บ
 บ        compliment to you guys.  On the contrary, according to Perfect      บ
 บ        Form, Razor has been putting down Coredump for releasing Quake.     บ
 บ        Is Razor justified in its actions?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CD: Personally, I have a lot of respect for Razor because I have seen   บ
 บ        them stay in the scene forever.  They have been putting out some    บ
 บ        of the best games, and have lasted through many generations of      บ
 บ        groups.  So I can see where Razor is coming from when a new group   บ
 บ        such as Coredump beats them to a big release such as Quake.  I do   บ
 บ        not put down Razor for this, because duping has been happening      บ
 บ        more often in the last year or so, and it is a major problem in     บ
 บ        the scene.  Razor has been a part of the scene for a long time,     บ
 บ        and could get the benefit of the doubt for that reason, which is    บ
 บ        unfortunate.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: So, you are saying that Razor duped Coredump, but most people will  บ
 บ        still believe that Coredump duped Razor because Razor is the older  บ
 บ        group?  Do you have any proof that Razor's release of Quake was a   บ
 บ        dupe?  After all, Razor's release of Quake was uploaded to all the  บ
 บ        major boards.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CD: Yes, that's what I am saying.  Although Razor may not admit it,     บ
 บ        most releases are taken care of on the Internet these days, and     บ
 บ        our release was on all the major sites first.  So it really comes   บ
 บ        down to the question, do boards or sites decide if a release is a   บ
 บ        dupe or not?  In the past, boards have been the key to judging      บ
 บ        whether a release is a dupe or not, but as the scene changes, so    บ
 บ        should the deciding factors.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: You also mentioned that dupes is becoming a much bigger problem in  บ
 บ        the scene lately, how does Coredump prevent itself from duping?     บ
 บ        And if/when Coredump does dupe, what is its immediate policy        บ
 บ        concerning the matter?                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CD: Well, we would obviously dupe check extensively.  We would usually  บ
 บ        also take our time and make sure that no other groups are going to  บ
 บ        release the same thing.  If we do dupe, we will admit it.  If we    บ
 บ        win on a release, we are not going to cower into a corner just      บ
 บ        because a much more established group releases the same thing.  We  บ
 บ        stand by our releases.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: You described Razor as good group earlier because Razor has been    บ
 บ        in the scene for many "generations."  What do you mean by           บ
 บ        "generations" when you use that word to describe Razor?             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CD: I meant that Razor has lasted through many other overpowering       บ
 บ        groups such as INC, THG, Genesis, TDU-JAM!, etc.  Razor has         บ
 บ        managed to remain prominent and competitive through all the other   บ
 บ        legacies of game release groups.                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What are your future hopes and plans for Coredump?  How many        บ
 บ        generations do you believe Coredump will last before it either      บ
 บ        merges into another group or dies off?                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CD: Coredump hopes to establish itself as a quality releasing power in  บ
 บ        the scene, and to continue releasing good games.  I can't tell      บ
 บ        right now how long we will last, but we won't be short lived.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Turok                บ
 บ    Subject  : AOD+LGT=More LGT          Affiliation : Lightning Senior     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: I recently found that the courier group Lightning has nearly        บ
 บ        doubled in size in a short week, what was the cause of this?        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ LGT: Yes, about 3 days ago, AOD (Angles of Death) merged with Lightning  บ
 บ        to cause an increase in members.                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Why did AOD decide to merge into Lightning?  Why did this merge     บ
 บ        happen, how long has this merged been planned before it was taken   บ
 บ        into effect?                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ LGT: Well, from what I know, AOD decided to merge due to the fact that   บ
 บ        they weren't getting noticed by the scene and weren't couriering    บ
 บ        enough to keep them as a group.  The merge happened because they    บ
 บ        had no place to go or couldn't move forward because they weren't    บ
 บ        competing with any other of the courier groups in the scene.  I     บ
 บ        think it was planned a few days in advance.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: You are now a senior member of Lightning, were you a senior before  บ
 บ        the merge?  Were you a leader in AOD when AOD merged into           บ
 บ        Lightning, or have you always been a member of Lightning?           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ LGT: Well, when I started in Lightning, I started as an IRC              บ
 บ        Coordinator, which was a senior postion, and yes, I was a senior    บ
 บ        when the merge occured.  I wasn't really a part in helping make     บ
 บ        the merge take place.  Darksoul had a major role with getting the   บ
 บ        merge to happen.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How has Lightning's role in the scene changed since the merge?      บ
 บ        Has the merge made Lightning a more respectable courier group?      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ LGT: The merge has made Lightning a more powerful couriering force in    บ
 บ        the scene.  Before the merge, we lacked couriers, and this merge    บ
 บ        has brought us more couriers which means we'll be doing a better    บ
 บ        job on sites and offering.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How did the merge take place, were all AOD couriers accepted into   บ
 บ        Lightning, or did very few AOD couriers make it into Lightning?     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ LGT: Most of the couriers made it into Lightning, the people who didn't  บ
 บ        want to merge were given a chance to join, but there were very few  บ
 บ        people who didn't want to merge, so we gained a lot of new          บ
 บ        couriers out of the merge.  The merge was decided in channel #AOD   บ
 บ        where all the decisions were made.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Were there any ex-AOD seniors or leaders that are now leaders in    บ
 บ        Lightning?  Or was this strictly a group takeover, where Lightning  บ
 บ        absorbed AOD?  In other words, do ex-AOD seniors or leaders have a  บ
 บ        say in what goes on in Lightning?                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ LGT: No, the highest postion that any of the AOD members got were        บ
 บ        coordinators, and senior FTP/IRC traders, but most of them became   บ
 บ        couriers and a few artist also.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: You freely claim that Lightning is now a new powerful force in the  บ
 บ        scene, but what can Lightning do to back up the scene's             บ
 บ        expectations?  What makes Lightning different from the various      บ
 บ        courier groups out there, what makes Lightning stand out?           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ LGT: Well, now that we have more man power, we're more able to           บ
 บ        acomplish more goals and standards.  Lightning has been             บ
 บ        reoraganized since the merge and is ready to show what it can do.   บ
 บ        We're different because of the fact that we have experienced        บ
 บ        leaders and couriers.  Most of our seniors and highers are from     บ
 บ        various different groups in the IBM/PC scene which makes them very  บ
 บ        experienced and some have also run their own gorups at one time.    บ
 บ        I think the name and the names of the people running the group      บ
 บ        makes the group stand out even more.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What are the future plans for Lightning?  Is Lightning planning to  บ
 บ        head up its own offer channel modeling itself after groups such as  บ
 บ        FATE (Fast Action Trade Exchange) and Motiv8, or is Lightning       บ
 บ        planning to stick to board/site couriering, thus modeling itself    บ
 บ        after groups such as Amnesia and RISC (Rise in Superior             บ
 บ        Couriering)?                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ LGT: For now, I don't think Lightning is going to open a leech channel   บ
 บ        due to the fact that most members don't want one and also because   บ
 บ        there's no to have one.  Those channels only help to try and get    บ
 บ        the group more respect, by having an offer channel, which I think   บ
 บ        is a waste of time and energy since there are so many now.  We're   บ
 บ        planning to get into more serious FTP sites and get up on the FTP   บ
 บ        charts.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: The FTP charts, to what are you referring to?                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ LGT: Well, everyone knows that RCN displays the best couriers on the     บ
 บ        Internet, and so Lightning would like to get up there on the RCN    บ
 บ        charts.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  The AOD - Lightning Merge                                                 บ
 บ  -------------------------                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There have been some questions about the Angels of Death (AOD) and    บ
 บ  Lightning merge.  I hope to answer some of these questions in the         บ
 บ  following paragraphs.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Because of school and other commitments, Nightsky, President of AOD,  บ
 บ  felt he could not give the group the stable leadership that it deserves.  บ
 บ  However, he did not want to see the group, that he and others worked so   บ
 บ  hard to establish, just die and be forgotten.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Fearing that the group might die after losing the strong leadership   บ
 บ  of Nightsky and Morbid, who left because of personal reasons, the option  บ
 บ  of merging into Lightning was presented to the members.  After a lengthy  บ
 บ  discussion, a vote was taken and 75% of the AOD membership voted to       บ
 บ  merge into Lightning.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There was a general consensus that Lightning has strong, stable       บ
 บ  leadership and an excellent Internet team, while AOD has excellent FTP    บ
 บ  and BBS divisions.  Combining the two groups will make Lightning an       บ
 บ  unstopable force in the scene.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      When asked about the merge and what it will do for Lightning,         บ
 บ  Darksoul, the Lightning President said, "It is the best move that both    บ
 บ  groups could have made.  It gives us (Lightning) what we have been        บ
 บ  lacking for the last few weeks and makes us even stronger than ever       บ
 บ  before.  We now have stronger leadership (if that's possible), an         บ
 บ  improved IRC/FTP division, and an absolutely oustanding BBS division.  I  บ
 บ  look for us to be one of the top courier groups very very soon!"          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Nightsky had the following to say about the merge, "I hope, thanks    บ
 บ  to the input of the AOD couriers and members, that Lightning will be a    บ
 บ  ruling force in the scene in a short time."                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Mystic One                บ

 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : Airwalk              บ
 บ    Subject  : CCA Overview              Affiliation : CCA President        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How did CCA (Central Crime Association) come about?  When did you   บ
 บ        decide to start your courier group CCA?                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CCA: Well, I decided to start CCA after THC (The Hardened Criminals)     บ
 บ        decided to go on as a release group.  CCA was brought up powerful,  บ
 บ        and still is powerful.  CCA started on the 28th of June.  CCA       บ
 บ        started small and is growing bigger and more influential as a       บ
 บ        couriering force everyday.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What experience do you have as a leader and member of groups?       บ
 บ        Have you ever held leadership positions in other courier groups?    บ
 บ        How experienced are you as a leader?  And what can you do as a      บ
 บ        leader that no one else can?                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CCA: Well, I was senior in THC, and I have a big past of affiliations.   บ
 บ        I have seen a lot of people manage, and I try to mimic their ways.  บ
 บ        I do it my way as well, but I use a little bit of every leader I    บ
 บ        have been around.  There is really not much I can do that no one    บ
 บ        else can do except for leading very well.  I consider myself a      บ
 บ        good leader and I think my group does too because I keep things     บ
 บ        organized 100% and so on.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How is CCA managed, are you the sole leader of CCA?  And how do     บ
 บ        you keep things in CCA 100% organized?                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CCA: CCA is managed by me and the CCA Council.  Seniors take a little    บ
 บ        part in it as well.  CCA is organized in teams.  We have teams      บ
 บ        taking 2 sites or more, those teams just focus on those sites.      บ
 บ        For example, Team A takes on the WHQ and the US-HQ, team B takes    บ
 บ        on the EHQ and the Norway HQ, team C takes on two other distro      บ
 บ        sites, and so on.  There are 4 teams in CCA, they each are          บ
 บ        dedicated, and willing.  I am just around to keep everyone inline,  บ
 บ        and working.  If they don't work and I have no use for them, they   บ
 บ        get kicked out.  I have a lot of good and dedicated people like     บ
 บ        Toosmooth, the CCA Vice President, and Fabfive a very good council  บ
 บ        member, and Dupe, who all play very big rolls in CCA.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Your team seems to be presented very well, how did you come about   บ
 บ        with such a strong team?                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CCA: It sort of came about as Midhack's idea.  Midhack is a very good    บ
 บ        courier, and he has alot of good ideas, and his idea really helped  บ
 บ        out CCA with me modifying his idea.  Midhack is also CCA's Head     บ
 บ        Courier.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: In making CCA a good courier group, it must be doing something      บ
 บ        that makes it special or extraordinary, what might that be?  What   บ
 บ        makes CCA different from the myriad of other courier groups out     บ
 บ        there?  What separates it from being second class?                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CCA: CCA isn't like any other courier group because we are mainly made   บ
 บ        up of friends and leaders.  What I would think of CCA that makes    บ
 บ        it special is its name Central Crime Association.  CCA is sort of   บ
 บ        a gang, not a courier group.  It's just a group of people hanging   บ
 บ        out supporting the warez community, we try as much as possible to   บ
 บ        get our warez to the public, we don't just trade among ourselves,   บ
 บ        we also trade with public people.  And that's the truth.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: I never said you lied.  Anyway, are there any plans for CCA to      บ
 บ        start up its own offer channel following the footsteps of groups    บ
 บ        such as FATE (Fast Action Trade Exchange) and Motiv8?               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ CCA: We already have an offer channel shared with other courier groups.  บ
 บ        We ran #THCfiles until THC died.  What a bummer, and now, CCA       บ
 บ        started and other groups started a thing called CrimeXnet, our      บ
 บ        offer channel is in channel #Xnet, a very good offer channel        บ
 บ        indeed.  CCA's offer team frequents there very well.  However, our  บ
 บ        IRC Head Courier, manages all the things that pass through #Xnet,   บ
 บ        he is CCA's representative for #Xnet, and the other groups have     บ
 บ        their representatives as well.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Ravan                     Interviewee : FBI Boy              บ
 บ    Subject  : Razor DUPES on Quake!?    Affiliation : Coredump Senior      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What is your view on the Razor/Coredump release of Quake last       บ
 บ        week?                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ FBI: Razor duped.  It was close, but Coredump beat Razor to the boards   บ
 บ        and to the Internet.  Rumors went around that the Coredump release  บ
 บ        of Quake did not work, but that is not true.  People only say that  บ
 บ        because while we were spreading Quake, one of the copies had 3      บ
 บ        disks screwed up and they where distributed incorrectly to several  บ
 บ        popular sites.  Those disks have since been deleted and replaced    บ
 บ        by working ones.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: You claim that Coredump beat Razor to the boards AND the Internet?  บ
 บ        I've been hearing that Coredump beat Razor to the Internet, but     บ
 บ        NOT on boards, can you explain this?                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ FBI: Razor got it to their boards before we did, but we got it to A      บ
 บ        board first.  We also got it to the FTP sites LA and BBX before     บ
 บ        Razor had it on ANY board.  I personally have nothing against       บ
 บ        Razor and I think that they are a GREAT group, but they lost on     บ
 บ        this one.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Ok, but do you acknowledge that Razor won on the Internet, even     บ
 บ        though a release is usually judged by who gets it on the boards     บ
 บ        first?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ FBI: No, Razor definitely lost on the Internet.  You may see it on a     บ
 บ        few sites because the siteops don't have the balls to delete a      บ
 บ        Razor release.  Plain and simple.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How many disks of the Coredump release made it to the Internet by   บ
 บ        the time Razor put one disk up?                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ FBI: All of them.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: REALLY???                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ FBI: Yes.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: I have tested the Coredump version of Quake.  It's very good and I  บ
 บ        have found no bugs, at least not yet, but it took me forever to     บ
 บ        find.  However, I could find the Razor version everywhere, why      บ
 บ        would this be if Coredump's version was uploaded first and Razor's  บ
 บ        version is a dupe?  Wouldn't the siteops nuke Razor's version       บ
 บ        since it was a dupe?                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ FBI: The reason for that is because most siteops don't know about        บ
 บ        Coredump and they do know Razor.  So they go with Razor because     บ
 บ        they don't know any better.  Most siteops don't have the balls to   บ
 บ        nuke a Razor release.  They just think that Razor is perfect        บ
 บ        quality and that they never dupe.  Also, Coredump's reputation has  บ
 บ        had a checkered past so siteops that do know about Coredump are     บ
 บ        apprehensive to leave ours on and nuke Razor's.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Are you referring to the uncracked NHL Power Play released by       บ
 บ        Coredump as the checkered past?                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ FBI: Yup...                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: If you did dupe Razor, and I'm not saying you did, then why did     บ
 บ        you do it?                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ FBI: We did NOT dupe Razor!  If you think so, you are WRONG!  We had it  บ
 บ        first and I believe Razor has come to terms with it somewhat        บ
 บ        though they are still upset they were beat.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Also, this may seem strange, but there seems to be a Napalm         บ
 บ        file.diz in the Coredump release of Quake, can you tell me why?     บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Fairchild                 Interviewee : Dee                  บ
 บ    Subject  : Core Steals the Credit?   Affiliation : NGT President        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: In RCN #24, Stank-e makes the claim that the offering channel       บ
 บ        #Phatfiles was started and controlled mainly by Core.  It became    บ
 บ        obvious that soon after, NGT (Next Generation Traders) became       บ
 บ        angry about what he said, why is that?                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ NGT: Because of the fact that he claims Core started it, when they did   บ
 บ        not.  This has happened several times, I don't put all of this      บ
 บ        hard work in for nothing.  I offered everyday when it opened, and   บ
 บ        asked all my friends to also.  I made it what it is today, and      บ
 บ        Core jumped on the bandwagon after channel #Phatfiles was already   บ
 บ        well established.  NGT members have gotten none of the credit for   บ
 บ        all our hard work.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Core and NGT still have gotten along great, from what I have seen,  บ
 บ        does this threaten Core/NGT relations in any way?  If so, what do   บ
 บ        you plan on doing about it?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ NGT: I have nothing against Core, but shit like this gets me pissed      บ
 บ        off.  Core members have been setting topics in channel #Phatfiles   บ
 บ        that make it seem like they own it, "[Core] Phatfiles [Core]."  I   บ
 บ        like to keep the channel a non-group based channel, like neutral    บ
 บ        grounds.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: In a previous issue, you say that RCN may have played a small part  บ
 บ        in leading people to believe that channel #Phatfiles was run by     บ
 บ        Core, can you explain how that is exactly?                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ NGT: Well, previously in RCN in the Warez-IQ Quiz, you guys made a       บ
 บ        screw up in the question that asked who runs channel #Phatfiles.    บ
 บ        You then listed Core, FATE (Fast Action Trade Exchange), and        บ
 บ        Motiv8 as the answers, and Core being the right one.  The channel   บ
 บ        isn't run by Core, like channel #Exceed is run by FATE and channel  บ
 บ        #M8Leech is run by Motiv8, channel #Phatfiles is made up of         บ
 บ        several groups.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Stank-e claims that Palm, who used to run channel #M8Leech,         บ
 บ        decided to start the channel #Phatfiles.  He also claims that       บ
 บ        because Palm was in Core at the time, Core runs the channel, what   บ
 บ        do you have to say about that?                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ NGT: Core, NGT, and the other groups run it now, but NGT started it.     บ
 บ        Primarily, me and Palm started it.  I brought the DCC offering      บ
 บ        people and Palm ran the bots, that's how it should be known.        บ
 บ        However, Stank-e is making this very hard, by spreading             บ
 บ        misinformation.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Well, thank you for your time, and for giving your side of the      บ
 บ        story Dee.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ NGT: No, thank you.  I hope this interview will clear up all the         บ
 บ        misinformation out there spread by Stank-e.  :)                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Everybody in the 416 and 905 area codes should be keeping a look out  บ
 บ  for a while.  I've heard from two reliable sources that the RCMP (Royal   บ
 บ  Canadian Mounted Police) is hitting Toronto hard.  Beyond Akira, a        บ
 บ  bulletin board run by Pharaoh of Razor 1911, was busted on the morning    บ
 บ  of the 30th of July.  Here are a few anonymous comments I held with some  บ
 บ  people about it.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Digitex> Can I get some information on Beyond Akira being busted?  I     บ
 บ            hear it was the RCMP and I see that the Beyond Akira nodes and  บ
 บ            telnet are down.                                                บ

 บ            situation as of yet?                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ         think they are being worked on. I am just finding the information  บ
 บ         as it comes, but it was verified about 2 to 3 minutes ago.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Digitex> Where is your information coming from?                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Anon> This information is from a reliable source in the 416/905 area     บ
 บ         codes.  Well, if you want some more information, the RCMP formed   บ
 บ         a group a few months ago to stop the piracy in Canada.  6 months   บ
 บ         ago in Montreal, 12 boards went down, some time after that, they   บ
 บ         formed the coalition, and now as it looks, they are hitting        บ
 บ         Toronto.  There are always busts of this nature around here.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Digitex> Where can I find some information about this RCMP coalition?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Anon> Well, I don't know about that much about the coalition, but the    บ
 บ         RCMP formed something a few months ago to try to end the piracy.   บ
 บ         All the elites of 416/905 should keep an eye out though.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Digitex> When the RCMP raided Beyond Akira, do you know how much warez   บ
 บ            was found?                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ          am not sure as to the exact meggage, but the information about    บ
 บ          the 140 gigs was leaked out by a X-Force Senior, so I do not      บ
 บ          know first hand.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, that's it for the comments.  Here are some of my own            บ
 บ  speculations on this.  If it's true that the RCMP is coming down on       บ
 บ  Toronto as hard as it seems, then the 416 and 905 area codes had REALLY   บ
 บ  better watch out.  I realize that it's sometimes much more difficult to   บ
 บ  bust smaller boards, but at the same time, they are all run by people,    บ
 บ  and the RCMP or FBI or whatever can get to them just as easily.  So, if   บ
 บ  you're running a board in the 416 or 905 area codes, I highly suggest     บ
 บ  you lay low for a while.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  How Did Trite Get the RCN Compiler?                                       บ
 บ  -----------------------------------                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Only Xenon, Hitex, and I were supposed to have been given access to   บ
 บ  copies of the RCN compiler.  However, near the demise of the first RCN    บ
 บ  at issue 13, Road Rebel was made an editor of RCN and was thus given a    บ
 บ  copy of the RCN compiler to continue RCN's legacy.  Road Rebel then       บ
 บ  asked Entropy to help run RCN with him because they were good friends at  บ
 บ  the time.  Since Entropy would also be considered an editor, he too       บ
 บ  received a copy of the RCN compiler from Road Rebel.  However, a few      บ
 บ  weeks later, Entropy uh.. "broke up" with Road Rebel, and their           บ
 บ  relationship has failed since.  After their break up, Entropy has never   บ
 บ  stopped harrassing Road Rebel.  As far as I am aware, Entropy continues   บ
 บ  to harrass Road Rebel daily by doing immature IRC acts to Road Rebel      บ
 บ  here and there.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In these last couple weeks, to stand up for Road Rebel against        บ
 บ  Entropy's immature acts, I too it upon myself to make fun of Entropy by   บ
 บ  having Mad-RCN utter the words in my chipmunked voice (through Sound      บ
 บ  Blaster), "Entropy is a fag."  I called Entropy a fag because in many     บ
 บ  ways, he is a fag.  However, at present, he doesn't seem to be able to    บ
 บ  leave me alone either, and he constantly messages me on IRC, "Hi Rebel    บ
 บ  Chicken, you're my hero!"  I shutter to think of what Entropy messages    บ
 บ  to Road Rebel.  Road Rebel is too ashamed to mention them to me.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Anyhow, it also happens to be that Trite and Entropy live in the      บ
 บ  same area code, and they are good friends in real life.  So Entropy dug   บ
 บ  up the RCN compiler from months ago, and gave it to his friend Trite,     บ
 บ  who also happens to be a half decent coder.  Now, from this point on, I   บ
 บ  can only speculate that Entropy asked Trite to use the RCN compiler to    บ
 บ  make a fake RCN issue.  After all, Trite and Entropy here have access to  บ
 บ  a very secretive RCN compiler which they could use to make a very         บ
 บ  realistic looking RCN issue.  However, since Trite could not figure out   บ
 บ  how to use the RCN compiler, and it was of no use to either of them       บ
 บ  anymore, Trite simply trojaned/virused the RCN compiler and released it   บ
 บ  to the masses in an attempt to hurt RCN.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Needless to say, neither Trite nor Entropy will ever see the likes    บ
 บ  of the updated RCN compilers.  As a precaution, I then asked Hitex to     บ
 บ  give Entropy a phone call, and Hitex has taken care of everything since   บ
 บ  then.  And as a further precaution, I'll be snail mailing Entropy a       บ
 บ  little letter.  The content of the letter is of no relevance to anyone    บ
 บ  but Trite and Entropy.  However, if I do think my letter is funny, it'll  บ
 บ  find a spot in future publications the secret Mad-RCN.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In some ways, Trite and Entropy has taught RCN how to keep certain    บ
 บ  securities in a dimmer light, and thanks be to them.  However, Hitex and  บ
 บ  I have been comtemplating on releasing a public version of an older RCN   บ
 บ  compiler, and if we decide to do so, it'll of course, be a RCN compiler   บ
 บ  that is non trojaned/virused and should also contain interactive          บ
 บ  features that are an improvement on the one that is currently available.  บ
 บ  The current RCN compiler used is 1.2 megabytes zipped, and the            บ
 บ  trojaned/virused version released by Trite is approximately 128 kbs       บ
 บ  zipped.                                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ    Author  : Da Phreak                                                     บ
 บ    Subject : An Overview of Core                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Since there seems to be a large interest in the newly merged group    บ
 บ  Core, I would like to tell you some things about Core, opinions in Core,  บ
 บ  and future plans from 3 members of Core.  There will also be a fourth     บ
 บ  member, me, since I am also in Core, I will add my opinions where I feel  บ
 บ  necesarry.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  The Beginning                                                             บ
 บ  -------------                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Core started off as a merger between the two courier groups Total     บ
 บ  Kaos and Violation.  Core still has two presidents, Edge and Stank-e.     บ
 บ  Edge will explain the merger for us :                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <DaPhreak> What excactly caused the merger between Total Kaos and         บ
 บ             Violation?                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Edge> Well, we had similar members and we did the same shit, so I        บ
 บ         thought it'd be best if the two groups worked together.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A rather straight foward explanation, but it is the reason.  Core     บ
 บ  has been around for about 2 or 3 months now, and Core is making some      บ
 บ  waves in the hypothetical trading pool of the scene.  The IRC Team        บ
 บ  concept, thought up by Edge and Stank-e has been a massive help to        บ
 บ  channel #Phatfiles which is an offering channel for tons of other small   บ
 บ  courier groups.  Core also has very high expectations of their new        บ
 บ  members.                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Dallion> We keep up the tight screening process for new memebers so we   บ
 บ            can't just let everyone into the group.  Applicants must first  บ
 บ            prove themselves capable of being a part of Core.  This method  บ
 บ            has helped keep out all the 10 year old kids who just want to   บ
 บ            leech.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Core has moved up to the ranks of the other top courier groups.       บ
 บ  Core's top FTP courier SaltyDogg, has been consistently moving more and   บ
 บ  more megs each week.  He is averaging 500 megs per week, and is moving    บ
 บ  more and more each week.  This isn't behind the standards set by some of  บ
 บ  the other groups, and will get Core at the top of the heap in a short     บ
 บ  time.                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <DaPhreak> What, in your opinion, should be done in Core in order to      บ
 บ             make it one of the top courier groups?                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <SaltyDogg> I think Core needs to focus on moving warez and getting its   บ
 บ              name out in the scene more.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <DaPhreak> What are your opinions of the scene that Core has to reach?    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <SaltyDogg> I think that the scene has too many ego problems.  Everyone   บ
 บ              thinks that they are the best courier or that they are in     บ
 บ              the best group.  I believe that people like that should       บ
 บ              concentrate more on moving warez and releasing quality        บ
 บ              warez.                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I myself think that people in the scene do have ego problems.         บ
 บ  Nobody likes to see these petty arguments such as, "We are better, your   บ
 บ  group is nothing but full of lamers!"  But I mean, RCN points out when a  บ
 บ  group outright messes up at something, and that's acceptable, but I       บ
 บ  don't think that the people writing letters to RCN should use their       บ
 บ  letters as an instigator for some of these fights.  RCN is here to        บ
 บ  congratulate the people who are working hard and to point out the things  บ
 บ  that people do wrong.  I feel that this article should be informative to  บ
 บ  those who have not yet heard of Core, and it should also be informative   บ
 บ  to those who are set out on starting their own courier group.  This       บ
 บ  above was not just 3 short interviews, but rather, it was a collection    บ
 บ  of quotes from interviews which I employed.  The rest of the article is   บ
 บ  going to be written using the information I gained from the intervews.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Core is one of the few young courier groups out there that is         บ
 บ  showing potential in its ability to stay alive.  Core won't just          บ
 บ  disappear from the scene in a few weeks, it's here, and it's here to      บ
 บ  stay.  Core's IRC Team concept will revolutionize the way the average     บ
 บ  downloader will receive his or her warez.  The planned 24/7 bots, 5 to    บ
 บ  10 bots on each team, focusing on separate categories (i.e. 0 day,        บ
 บ  games/utils) offering in channel #Phatfiles will definitely help Core     บ
 บ  change the way the end users get warez.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Core is made up of a team of dedicated couriers, not a group made up  บ
 บ  of inactive members or leechers that don't play a "team game."  Core has  บ
 บ  an intricate working team, yes a team.  Everyone has a job, and they do   บ
 บ  that job.  If someone doesn't perform up to par, a new person will get a  บ
 บ  chance to do that job.  Core has a lot of IRC couriers, I know that       บ
 บ  because I am one of them.  But, IRC is where you are at.  This is what    บ
 บ  you guys want, and Core stands behind it.  Core stands behind the whole   บ
 บ  concept of mass couriering.  Distribution.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Anonymous                                                     บ
 บ    Subject : My Experience with Abe Ingersoll                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      First off, I won't incriminate myself in this article (I take the     บ
 บ  5th!), but I will explain my little experience with almost being busted.  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In November of last year, I, along with a couple friends were         บ
 บ  implicated by a 15 year old fuck by the name of Abe Ingersoll in Peoria,  บ
 บ  Illinois.  He goes by a few handles on IRC, namely ^abe^, possibly        บ
 บ  ^pest^ (his alias is pestilence, and no, not anyone in the scene that we  บ
 บ  all know of).  His host almost always includes "*!*ingers*."  If you      บ
 บ  know him, ban/kick/kill him (literally) or something.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Anyway, he was caught basically red-handed with numerous credit card  บ
 บ  receipts, carded merchandise, and t-philez about carding and shit.        บ
 บ  Well, in order to save his own little ass, we were implicated.  With us   บ
 บ  being local and all, and the cops freaking out about all the shit they    บ
 บ  found (mainly all the t-philez), me and a friend suddenly found           บ
 บ  ourselves called to the cop shop for "our version" of the story.          บ
 บ  Luckily, we knew what was happening and talked beforehand in great        บ
 บ  detail about everything (minus the 15 year old fuck).  I was straight     บ
 บ  with the cop when I told him that I'd been through the whole "gestapo     บ
 บ  interrogation" before, and to skip it.  I really wasn't in the mood for   บ
 บ  a pig to be yelling in my face that day.  In turn, he told me that I      บ
 บ  would not be placed under arrest today (bah, yeah right, like I haven't   บ
 บ  been told that before or nothing), and gave me a smoke.  :)               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Ok, I thought, he's going to go the "I'm your friend" route with me.  บ
 บ  Mr. Pig talked in detail about how he had already talked with the FBI,    บ
 บ  but the Secret Service were the ones who liked to handle computer         บ
 บ  crimes, and they were debating whether to pick up the investigation.      บ
 บ  The cops had information that could've only been gained through Abe or a  บ
 บ  phone tap.  Anyway, to make a long story short, I talked with the cop,    บ
 บ  and my friend got the "gestapo" route (sucked to be him).  Another        บ
 บ  interesting note is that my friend talked to the cops first.  The cop     บ
 บ  actually told him that *I* had already told him (the cop) all about how   บ
 บ  he (my friend) was the guilty party BEFORE I even talked to the cops!     บ
 บ  My friend knew better through our constant communication, kept his cool,  บ
 บ  and stuck to our story.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The cop was right though, I wasn't arrested, in fact, no one but the  บ
 บ  15 year old was.  Nothing about warez ever entered the picture.           บ
 บ  However, I do suspect that my phone along with my friend's phone was      บ
 บ  tapped at one point in time, and my friend actually did have a white van  บ
 บ  with green-G plates tail him for a few days.  From what I understand,     บ
 บ  the 15 year old has already been through the court thing, and got         บ
 บ  probation or something, because I just saw him on IRC the other day.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now, all the time this kid was carding, he kept saying, "Oh, I'm      บ
 บ  only 15, the worst they can do to me is put me in juvie until I'm 18."    บ
 บ  I explained to him several times that I was already on Intense Probation  บ
 บ  for felony convictions, and that if I was arrested, I'd go to the joint   บ
 บ  for several years, and he would be dead once I got out.  Unfortunately,   บ
 บ  that didn't stop him from rolling over on me for one second.  So, to put  บ
 บ  it all in perspective :                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.) If you're of legal age, NEVER trust a minor.  NEVER NEVER NEVER!  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.) If you're already on probation, stick to warez, much safer.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3.) NEVER talk on the phone about anything illegal if there's even a  บ
 บ          remote reason to suspect your line is tapped, better safe than    บ
 บ          sorry!                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      4.) I might be mistaken, but I believe that FedEx is still            บ
 บ          considered a private company.  Meaning that if you use them to    บ
 บ          ship your carded stuff, you can't be busted for mail fraud as     บ
 บ          well if/when you do get busted.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      5.) If you are called in for questioning, keep your wits about you,   บ
 บ          and remember that cops will *LIE* to manipulate you into          บ
 บ          thinking exactly what they want you to think.  Stick to your      บ
 บ          story, or call a lawyer.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      6.) One more thing, if the FBI/Secret Service is called in, you are   บ
 บ          basically FUCKED.  They have the power to really do anything      บ
 บ          they want, legal or otherwise.  They have the resources and       บ
 บ          tools to place bugs, laser listeners, and shit you've never       บ
 บ          heard of.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ    Author  : Airwalk                                                       บ
 บ    Subject : Microsoft Busts Airman!?                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป

 บ  ######### Windows NT  Workstation 4.0 final Build 1381 ######             บ
 บ  #CCA Release                                                              บ
 บ  Installable from previous winnt version     Rate: 10/10+                  บ
 บ   and from dos.                                                            บ
 บ  ######### Windows NT  Workstation 4.0 final Build 1381 ######             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Supplied by <WITHELD>                                                     บ
 บ  Packed by <WITHEHLD>                                                      บ
 บ  Comments: Thanks for MS shipping WINNT wks final to <WITHELD>.            บ
 บ            Thanks for <WIthheld> contributing his winnt 4.0 final.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ            This is <WITHHELD> and you could find me in #cca in Efnet.      บ
 บ            /away I am always away and will never be back.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ            Packed at #CCA <WITHHELD>, HQ, <WITHHELD, <WITHHELD> 4XXXX      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Sponsored by Student Judicial Affair at <WITHHELD> University             บ
 บ               University Technology Service at <WITHHELD University        บ
 บ               UNITS at <WITHEHLD> University                               บ
 บ               #CCA in Efent                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Note: MS release day:07/31/1996                                           บ
 บ         at <WITHELD> release day: 08/02/1996                               บ
 บ        #cca release day: 08/02/1996                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Disclaimer: This release of Winnt 4.0 final is for academic use only,     บ
 บ  If you need winnt workstation 4.0 final build 1381 for commercial use,    บ
 บ  contact Microsoft corporation.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The above was the nfo provided in the CCA release of Win NT v4.0      บ
 บ  Workstation.  The supplier, Airman, decided to release Win NT because     บ
 บ  all the releases out to date where pathetic too say the least (i.e. no    บ
 บ  drivers or you can't install from previous NT).  So he decided to grab a  บ
 บ  copy of NT from the University.  He (by himself) ripped it off the CD     บ
 บ  and packaged it around 2:00 am last night.  The 47 disk release was       บ
 บ  quickly spread and he went to bed thinking it was quite a success.  At    บ
 บ  this time, I too went to sleep as well not thinking much of it, but I     บ
 บ  was shocked when I came onto IRC the next day.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It seems that Microsoft (within a few hours of the relesae) got       บ
 บ  ahold of a copy of this release.  Living up to Microsoft's reputation,    บ
 บ  Microsoft emailed someone at the University requesting more information   บ
 บ  on the supplier.  This email had the file_id.diz attatched to it to show  บ
 บ  proof of the grounds of their claims.  I haven't seen this email, but I   บ
 บ  was assured that it was LEGIT.  The folks at the University now had to    บ
 บ  uncover what exactly happened (not knowing who or what Airman is).  I     บ
 บ  was told that they are working on finding out who he is, and that they    บ
 บ  are also complying with Microsoft's requests for more information on him  บ
 บ  to their best efforts.  No one has seen Airman since last night, and the  บ
 บ  outcome of this towards him has yet to be finalized.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Airman is most likely a free man now, and hopefully, he will stay     บ
 บ  that way throughout this Microsoft investigation.  Microsoft seems to     บ
 บ  want to bust this guy who never released anything before, instead of      บ
 บ  going after higher end "law-breakers."  This is quite a shame (Hi         บ
 บ  Microsoft, I know you're reading this!) for this was not a very           บ
 บ  offensive crime.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      To my knowledge, NO one knows exactly who he is besides seeing him    บ
 บ  on IRC.  This includes personel at the University in question.  And no    บ
 บ  further word, again, to my knowledge, has been sent from Microsoft.  All  บ
 บ  I can say is that people should beware... Microsoft is fast and furious   บ
 บ  about this.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
