 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Round Man                                                     บ
 บ    Subject : 5 Years from Present                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This article is strictly the opinion of one person based upon my      บ
 บ  experiences both as a BBS sysop and a long-time resident of the           บ
 บ  Internet.  Before you lock-and-load your industrial strength flame        บ
 บ  thrower, keep in mind that I'm wearing my asbestos boxer shorts.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Not that many years ago, 95% of us had two ways of trading our        บ
 บ  favorite warez goodies.  Most of our ill-gotten booty came from a small   บ
 บ  cadre of friends and aquaintances during coffee-break trading sessions    บ
 บ  or at the weekly AD&D game.  We could also get the occasional ware from   บ
 บ  our local, semi-legitimate BBSes.  If we were really lucky, we had a      บ
 บ  friend-of-a-friend that knew somebody that got us an account on a pirate  บ
 บ  board where we could leech to our heart's content until we had either     บ
 บ  maxxed out our 270 meg hard drive or sucked up everything they had to     บ
 บ  offer.  I didn't know anyone with access to the really BIG boards, but I  บ
 บ  was aware of their existance.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The Internet back in those days was the playground of academia, the   บ
 บ  government and a fortunate few who's companies used the Internet for      บ
 บ  transferring files between distant sites.  At that time, gopher was       บ
 บ  about as sophisticated as it got.  FTP was quite popular, but if there    บ
 บ  was a warez scene back then, it was well-hidden and not well organized.   บ
 บ  Since few PC owners had access, most of the interest was in UNIX          บ
 บ  programs and utilities.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Those were the glory days of the BBS scene.  The big boards were the  บ
 บ  lifeblood of distribution then, and anything worth leeching was in that   บ
 บ  channel.  Files were relatively small and you could download even the     บ
 บ  best stuff in a single evening at 2400 bps.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Those days are gone.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      We stand now at the threshold, the nexus between two realities.  The  บ
 บ  big boards are still popular and important to the scene, but the          บ
 บ  emphasis is slowly shifting away from them and toward the free-wheeling   บ
 บ  world of the Internet.  The days of the iron fisted control, exclusive    บ
 บ  access and long distance calling are over.  We have tasted the wild west  บ
 บ  flavor of the Internet, we've enjoyed its anonymity, and we will not go   บ
 บ  back.                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Many of you will object to this line of reasoning, some vehemently,   บ
 บ  but consider this, with each day that goes by, more people gain access    บ
 บ  the Internet and few ever log on to their local BBSes.  This trend shows  บ
 บ  no sign of weakening and for good reason.  With an Internet account, Joe  บ
 บ  Public can access everything on the Internet, no exceptions.  Exposure    บ
 บ  to illicit software is almost guaranteed for anyone who spends any        บ
 บ  serious time online.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Even the bastions of the BBS piracy scene have begrudgingly accepted  บ
 บ  the Internet as a necessary evil, allowing people to log on through       บ
 บ  telnet and using fast FTP sites as vehicles for mass storage and          บ
 บ  transfer.  As more and more users use telnet to access their favorite     บ
 บ  BBSes, modem banks will slowly come down while ISDN lines go up.  But     บ
 บ  more importantly, fewer users will choose to live within the constraints  บ
 บ  of the formal BBS, even by telnet.  More will choose to get their daily   บ
 บ  fix from anonymous FTP sites and DCC offer-bots because anyone can        บ
 บ  access them.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      That said, here are my prognostications, for what they're worth.      บ
 บ  Five years from today, this will be the state of the scene :              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.) BBSes will have faded from significance.  The number of 10+ node  บ
 บ          BBSes will be less than half of what we have now.  First release  บ
 บ          status will no longer be determined on BBSes.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.) The line between releasers and couriers will become much less     บ
 บ          distinct as powerful software will allow releasers to instantly   บ
 บ          distribute their warez to multiple sites concurrently.  Couriers  บ
 บ          will be relegated to the role of distributing to smaller,         บ
 บ          temporary, anonymous sites and DCC offerbots (or something more   บ
 บ          sophisticated).  That doesn't mean that they will be any less     บ
 บ          important to the scene, just further down the food chain.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3.) The 'rules' as we know them today will be just a fond memory.     บ
 บ          The number of short-lived groups will grow exponentially, as      บ
 บ          will their lack of respect for rules concerning dupes.  Although  บ
 บ          uncracked or poorly cracked warez will be far more common, there  บ
 บ          will always be a number of competing distributions, some of       บ
 บ          which are bound to work.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      4.) High-speed connections, rewritable CD-ROMs and more advanced      บ
 บ          high-capacity storage mechanisms will keep up with                บ
 บ          ever-increasing game and application sizes.  The escalation of    บ
 บ          the copy-protection wars will have continued, making crackers     บ
 บ          any group's most-valuable resource.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The basis of my predictions is my core philosophy - the purpose of    บ
 บ  the scene is to make usable software available to the end user.           บ
 บ  Anything that inhibits or runs counter to this reality is doomed to       บ
 บ  fail.  Any rule which does not honor this reality will be scoffed at and  บ
 บ  ignored.  Any group that does not observe this as their core purpose      บ
 บ  will be relegated to insignificant.                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Just one man's opinion.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ


                         ฐ
    ฿฿        ฐ       ฿฿฿ฐ                      ฐ฿฿฿
     ฿ ฿  ฿฿  ฿฿฿   ฿    ฿  r c n          ฿฿ ฿฿
   ฿ ฐ  ฿               ฿   ฿ฐ   ฿
 ฐ ฐฐ ฐ ฿ฐ ฐ฿ ฿ ฐ  ฿฿฿฿฿฿฿ ฐ ฐฐฐฐฐฐ ฐฐฐ
        ฿        ฐ฿฿฿฿฿฿   ฿       ฿

 บ    Author  : Frost                                                         บ
 บ    Subject : Napalm Disbands                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  The following is a letter by Prophet, leader of Napalm :                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hey!  I've really bad news for everyone!  I've decided to kill        บ
 บ  NAPALM.  As of now, it has been announced already.  Sorry guys, but I     บ
 บ  FUCKING LOVED NAPALM AND LOVED working with EVERYONE!!  I'm so sorry for  บ
 บ  this to happen.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Prophet                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It always saddens me to see a great group go down.  In Napalm's case  บ
 บ  especially since I was a part of it.  There will alway be those people    บ
 บ  that will try and tarnish the Napalm name saying that Napalm released     บ
 บ  non-working games and other bullshit.  The fact remains that Napalm was   บ
 บ  one of the best games release groups of its day.  And I'll be damned if   บ
 บ  I see another channel #Exceed lamer shoot off his mouth about something   บ
 บ  so much eliter than he could ever be.  I have a great deal of respect     บ
 บ  for Prophet and what he has set out to build.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Napalm was a good games group, and there is no debate to that.  In    บ
 บ  closing, I'd like to say that the scene suffers when a great group like   บ
 บ  Napalm goes down, and when Napalm went down, it took a little of the      บ
 บ  scene with it.  To Napalm!                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  <RblChickn> Really?                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ              Roulette.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> Oh well... to Napalm!                                         บ

 บ    Author  : Coupbird                                                      บ
 บ    Subject : Guild Merge                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As a founder of RTG (Rampant Trading Guild) and a head in the         บ
 บ  courier group Guild, I am writing this to let the scene know what we are  บ
 บ  all about.  The major goal of Guild is to help reform the warez scene,    บ
 บ  through excellence.  Our philosophy is very simple, we want to see the    บ
 บ  warez scene as a whole become better.  So how does Guild plan to do       บ
 บ  this?  The Guild has been formed with only the most dedicated couriers,   บ
 บ  skilled staff, and the best leadership around.  With that, we plan to     บ
 บ  create the highest level of warez trade ever!                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As we raise the playing field for couriering, the groups trying to    บ
 บ  catch up to Guilds' standards will also improve.  Resulting from this,    บ
 บ  the most efficient warez trade since the first pirated software title     บ
 บ  was released will be ushured.  If you are interested in joining the       บ
 บ  Guild team, join IRC Channel #Guild and pick up an app and nfo.  Only     บ
 บ  the best need apply.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ    Author  : Storm Hacker                                                  บ
 บ    Subject : Dam!  Where's TDU-JAM!?                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There are just so many new groups popping up these days.  Many of     บ
 บ  them being those "One Hit Wonders" type groups, and the other odd ones    บ
 บ  being the groups who make an impact on the scene.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I obtained an old release by the ever-famous game releasing group     บ
 บ  "TDU-JAM!"  This release was Destruction Derby.  As I read the group's    บ
 บ  nfo file, I just kept thinking to myself, why did this great group have   บ
 บ  to leave the scene?  Their nfo was always good and to the point.  Never   บ
 บ  any of that childish bullshit that would start a war between groups, and  บ
 บ  yet, their releases ALWAYS worked.  I don't think I ever got a copy of a  บ
 บ  TDU-JAM! release that didn't work.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Nowadays, we have groups which pop into the scene who come out with   บ
 บ  like 50 disk releases which turn out to be DEMOS or just some plain       บ
 บ  bullshit which nobody wants or needs.  And half the time, these releases  บ
 บ  do not work due to inproper ripping, cracking, or even just without       บ
 บ  supplying enough information on how to get the release to work.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There are some groups (very little) which do release quality          บ
 บ  releases, and do get the respect they deserve.  But there will always be  บ
 บ  the occasional 'bad' release, or dupe, which will cause a big scene in    บ
 บ  the scene (no pun intended).                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The only thing we need is for those who know how to do the job to do  บ
 บ  it, and for those who want to do it, to learn how to do it properly.      บ
 บ  Otherwise, don't even try.  I'm not trying to sound like a bastard or     บ
 บ  anything, but it's not worth our time and effort to download something    บ
 บ  that will not work (especially when it's 50+ disks big).  And it does     บ
 บ  hurt the scene.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Conway                                                        บ
 บ    Subject : The Oracle                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In ancient times, there was a thing called the Oracle, which was      บ
 บ  supposed to do wonderous things like healing the sick, blessing people    บ
 บ  with luck and predicting the future.  Today, a computer company named     บ
 บ  "Oracle" decided to predict the future itself.  Oracle is now developing  บ
 บ  a thing called a Web Box, which is a $500 TV-top add-on which connects    บ
 บ  to the Internet through cable or some other high-speed link.  The price   บ
 บ  is so low, because this unit will use the TV for a monitor, and have no   บ
 บ  hard disk at all.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Oracle sees this "appliance," as they like to call it, as the future  บ
 บ  of computers, and the one thing that will bring computers and             บ
 บ  couch-potatoes together.  Many skeptics foresee various futures for this  บ
 บ  enterprise.  A few say that the computer evolution will never allow       บ
 บ  itself to go back to the mainframe - a dumb terminal combination that     บ
 บ  was replaced once in the past.  Others predict that this is the end of    บ
 บ  PCs as we know it, and still more hope that both types of machines will   บ
 บ  peacefully coexist with the Boxes in the living room for entertainment,   บ
 บ  and the PCs in the den for real work.  I, personally, would like to       บ
 บ  belive the later version because the switch to Boxes could prove fatal    บ
 บ  to the scene.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      How would software companies sell their products to their "Boxed"     บ
 บ  customers?  Obviously on the server-client basis - meaning that the       บ
 บ  actual program will reside on the company's web server, and the client    บ
 บ  would purchase the right to use it from a particular box, or with a       บ
 บ  particular login name/password.  The development of such an arrangement   บ
 บ  is most profitable for the software companies because they WILL get paid  บ
 บ  for EVERY "copy" of their program used, and of course save lots of money  บ
 บ  on packaging and distribution.  But to the scene this would mean a        บ
 บ  certain, and quick death.  Since there's no way to use the program on a   บ
 บ  box unless you sign up with the company, there will be no possible way    บ
 บ  to use anything without paying for it!                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      What is that I hear you screaming?  Carding?  You forget that every   บ
 บ  box has a serial number, and as cable now, they would know the exact      บ
 บ  location of any cable jack you're currently using which will make         บ
 บ  carding an extremely unsafe game to play.  But that's the dark side.  It  บ
 บ  would be hard indeed for "The Box" to actually replace computers, but     บ
 บ  rather I believe, in the best case it will create a new market separate   บ
 บ  from the PC just like the Atari and Nintendo once did.  So have no fear,  บ
 บ  the scene days aren't numbered, yet...                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Killer                                                        บ
 บ    Subject : The Name Game                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It is sort of funny the names we put on people.  More specifically,   บ
 บ  the lack of names.  In the trading scene, we label people either "elite"  บ
 บ  or "lame."  Both of these titles are over used and ambiguous.  Every      บ
 บ  trader has at one time or another used these words to label someone.      บ
 บ  The fast traders use them, and ironically, the slow traders (who the      บ
 บ  fast traders call lame) also use both of these words.  But what do these  บ
 บ  words mean, if they mean anything anymore, and should they be used at     บ
 บ  all?                                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      What does the word "elite" mean anyway.  It can't describe someone    บ
 บ  who gets fast files.  When I was starting out, I called people that       บ
 บ  could get 1 month stuff "elite."  Now people that I know call people      บ
 บ  that get 0 day files "elite."  However, on IRC, anyone can join a         บ
 บ  "warez" channel and pick up fast files.  Does that makes you "elite?"     บ
 บ  The word "elite" might describe a person who has in depth knowledge of    บ
 บ  the trading scene.  But you can become knowledgeable about the scene      บ
 บ  with out ever trading a file (just read RCN).                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      "Elite" is a word that conveys respect.  It, however, is used too     บ
 บ  often.  Everyone is respected in the scene by someone else, all for       บ
 บ  different reasons.  One word is not adequate to describe the meanings of  บ
 บ  which people associate with the word "elite."  It is an outdated word.    บ
 บ  A word that should have been left behind with the 2400 and 14400 modems.  บ
 บ  A simple word for simple times.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The same holds true for the word "lame."  What makes someone "lame?"  บ
 บ  Are you "lame" if you can get fast files, or only if you can't get fast   บ
 บ  files but try to trade with people higher up in the scene than you.  Is   บ
 บ  speed the only factor in determining if a person is "lame" or not?  If    บ
 บ  this is so, then people that label people who get slower files "lame"     บ
 บ  are assholes.  We all (most of us), worked our way up the scene ladder,   บ
 บ  so we all were "lame" at one point in time.  We should then help out the  บ
 บ  people in the position that we were once in.  BUT "lame" is NOT just      บ
 บ  used to describe a person lower in the scene hierarchy.  It has been      บ
 บ  used to describe arrogant group leaders, whole groups even, people who    บ
 บ  look down on others, and so on.  So when in hell's name should someone    บ
 บ  be labeled "lame?"  In my opinion NEVER.  The word "lame" is again too    บ
 บ  broad, it means too much, and is used too often. It is a word that has    บ
 บ  no place in the scene of today.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      New labels must be created, labels that are more specific and         บ
 บ  meaningful.  We need labels that will make a person proud when called it  บ
 บ  by others or words that put an asshole in his place.  "Lame" and "elite"  บ
 บ  don't mean anything anymore.  It is time for a new set of lingo to grow   บ
 บ  and take its place.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In the real world, word change evolve with the culture that uses      บ
 บ  them over long periods of time.  "Cyberspace" changes much faster than    บ
 บ  any culture, but its lingo does not.  Only an effort on the part of us    บ
 บ  (trader/and others), will correct the annoying problem of outdated        บ
 บ  lingo.                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ฐ ฐฐ ฐ ฿ฐ ฐ฿ ฿ ฐ  ฿฿฿฿฿฿฿ ฐ ฐฐฐฐฐฐ ฐฐฐ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Digitex                                                       บ
 บ    Subject : Software Piracy                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hi guys!  I'm back, so I decided to start off with an article on      บ
 บ  software piracy and the pirate scene, and how the two of those combined   บ
 บ  effect everything else that goes on around us on the Internet.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Since the FBI has outlawed the previewing of software, it has become  บ
 บ  more and more difficult to find ways to get a warez BBS to stay up        บ
 บ  without arousing suspiscion (especially from the feds).  This article     บ
 บ  will discuss how to (almost) fed-proof your site, BBS, whatever as well.  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      We all know that the entrapment law forces any law enforcement or     บ
 บ  federal agency members to declare that they are indeed members of         บ
 บ  whatever agency they are affiliated with.  This means that if a site or   บ
 บ  BBS that a federal agent or law enforcer of any sort is applying for      บ
 บ  asks him/her if they are one of those, they MUST say yes or do whatever   บ
 บ  it requires them to do.  This is of course within reason, the BBS/Site    บ
 บ  can't really make the person jump up and down, light his/her hair on      บ
 บ  fire and run through the street yelling, "I'm a gerbil!  Don't eat my     บ
 บ  pickles!!!"  Such maybe reasonable would be to ask a Fed to hang up, or   บ
 บ  whatever.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There are other things in the disclaimer you should put, such as      บ
 บ  that you take no responsibility for what the users do with the files      บ
 บ  they download from your BBS/site, and many other things.  Use your        บ
 บ  creative imaginations!                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Another especially good way to protect your site or BBS from          บ
 บ  unwanted guests is to force them to upload something before allowing      บ
 บ  them access.  If the new user knows what kind of BBS/site this is, he     บ
 บ  will obviously send something pirated.  If the federal agent or law       บ
 บ  enforcer sends something pirated, he cannot bust you, since he is in      บ
 บ  violation of his own laws, and then he's pretty much fucked anyway.  If   บ
 บ  the person uploads something that is maybe public domain or shareware,    บ
 บ  just kick them off.  They probably wouldn't be any use to you anyway.     บ
 บ  Even in the event that somebody uploads something pirated to your         บ
 บ  BBS/site and you don't normally allow pirated software to be uploaded to  บ
 บ  your BBS/site, the law grants you 24 hours to check and delete it, since  บ
 บ  a sysop cannot be up at all hours of the day making sure that pirated     บ
 บ  software isn't being uploaded.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now, onto the part about piracy's effects to the world.  Piracy       บ
 บ  effects the world, or more aptly termed Internet, but some people         บ
 บ  consider it another world so I guess either is fine, in many ways, both   บ
 บ  good and bad.  It effects the REAL world in that it hurts software        บ
 บ  companies' profits and that it can get you busted if you're in the wrong  บ
 บ  part of the world such as the US, Canada, etc.  Its good effects are      บ
 บ  that since most software companies are either too lazy to release         บ
 บ  shareware/demos of their products or their shareware/demos are so         บ
 บ  crippled you cannot effectively evaluate the software, pirating provides  บ
 บ  a way for users to evaluate the software before they purchase it.  Of     บ
 บ  course, as I said before, this was outlawed.  Apparently, software        บ
 บ  companies are too greedy to care if their users will be able to use       บ
 บ  their software and that the software will suit their needs.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It's getting to the point that there are so many different programs   บ
 บ  out there, and so few reviews on those programs that only the huge        บ
 บ  megacorporations can effectively release shareware or demos.  This is     บ
 บ  also the same for reviews.  Only the large companies can get reviews      บ
 บ  from reputable magazines or whatnot.  So a smaller company that produces  บ
 บ  a product that is actually better than Microsoft's newest office          บ
 บ  management program may never get any sort of review or shareware copy     บ
 บ  released, and they will lose money from that.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In general, software costs too much for people to be going out and    บ
 บ  buying it left and right in case the program they bought first does not   บ
 บ  suit their needs.  Since most major stores don't allow trades of          บ
 บ  software, even of the same type, the person who bought the software is    บ
 บ  out of luck.  He's lost about $50 to $70 to some worthless software       บ
 บ  because he could not properly evaluate the software by looking at the     บ
 บ  colorful box prior to purchasing it.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      If the FBI is going to outlaw software piracy in the United States,   บ
 บ  why don't all countries do it?  That is a problem I cannot understand.    บ
 บ  The companies don't want people pirating their software, yet the people   บ
 บ  over in say, Amsterdam, can freely distribute it, since there's no FBI    บ
 บ  there, to my knowledge.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In closing, I'd just like to say that software DOES cost too much to  บ
 บ  be thrown around like it's such an unimportant, miniscule thing, and      บ
 บ  that the companies who are writing the software should find a better way  บ
 บ  to allow potential users to preview their software before wasting their   บ
 บ  money on something they possibly can't use.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Pele                                                          บ
 บ    Subject : USR Fucksters 33.6 v.34                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I recently purchased a USR Sporster 33.6 v.34 expecting to get it     บ
 บ  home and plug it in and start surfing.  I was severely mistaken.  I       บ
 บ  brought my modem home and opened the package.  I then set the com ports   บ
 บ  as instructed, etc.  Things seemed fine at first, then I started to       บ
 บ  notice that during my connections it would pause, or stop responding      บ
 บ  completely.  I assumed that this was caused by some fault of mine,        บ
 บ  possible init strings problems or something to that extent.  I fiddled    บ
 บ  with the init strings and com port settings for several hours and then    บ
 บ  decided that it would be better to try it the next day after I had some   บ
 บ  rest.                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      While I was at work the next day, I decided I would call the USR      บ
 บ  Tech Support to see if they had any ideas.  After listening to 7 minutes  บ
 บ  of recorded messages, I decided it wasn't worth running up the phone      บ
 บ  companies' bills.  I came home that evening and checked out the           บ
 บ  conference comp.dcom.modems and to my surprise, found more than 100       บ
 บ  messages detailing the same exact problem that I had.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I called the USR Tech Support and after 10 minutes on hold, I         บ
 บ  finally got "Jose" who seemed to have no technical knowlege other than    บ
 บ  the cue card that he was obviously holding in front of him.  He went      บ
 บ  through the obvious.  He asked me what kind of computer I was running.    บ
 บ  I told him that I have a DX2/66 with 8 megabytes of RAM.  He told me to   บ
 บ  make sure that I had com 1 disabled in my BIOS.  I so kindly informed     บ
 บ  him that there was no COM settings in a 486 board.  Then he asked me to   บ
 บ  go into MSD and check the com ports.  When he found out that my com1 was  บ
 บ  displaying a 2400 baud rate he said that my problem would be cured if I   บ
 บ  moved my modem to com3 and irq 5.  He also said again to disable my com   บ
 บ  port in my BIOS and when I again told him that my BIOS had no com         บ
 บ  settings, he insulted me by asking who built my computer.  I replied      บ
 บ  that I built the computer and he shut the fuck up.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So I hung up and switched my modem to com 3 irq 5 having to switch    บ
 บ  my Sound Blaster card to irq 7 and temporarily disabling my LPT port.     บ
 บ  This however did not resolve the problem.  Very upset, I called USR Tech  บ
 บ  Support yet again.  This time after waiting for only 15 minutes on a      บ
 บ  long distance connection, I was connected with "Magadababba mohababba     บ
 บ  abdul makharrah bushi" and he asked me the obvious.  When I told him      บ
 บ  that I had read over 100 messages detailing the same exact problem as I   บ
 บ  he asked my FirmWare (EPROM) date and I told him.  He then said I would   บ
 บ  have to send my modem in to have the EPROM upgraded.  I have read         บ
 บ  several messages from people on USENET who say that this has resolved     บ
 บ  their problems.  So, if you have a USR Sportster 33.6 v.34 with an EPROM  บ
 บ  date between 10/95 and 3/96 (you can find this out by typing ati7 at      บ
 บ  your terminal window) and you are having the "pausing" problem then I     บ
 บ  would recommend that you contact USR Tech Support at (847) 982-5151 and   บ
 บ  tell them that you need to have your EPROM upgraded.  This will be a      บ
 บ  free upgrade.  Please, if they hassle you, don't put up with it, ask to   บ
 บ  speak with their supervisor.  This is obviously a known problem and they  บ
 บ  have made no effort to correct this.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I hope that this has been a help, and if you are upset that I         บ
 บ  included the entire conversation and summary of events that took place,   บ
 บ  then please excuse me.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ

                                         ฿     r e v i e w s !

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 3 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ

                                         ฿     r e v i e w s !

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 3 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 3 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ GAME REVIEWS, RATINGS, UN-BIASED OPINIONS, HELP/TIPS FOR INSTALLING GAMES! บ
 บ [][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][] บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Rating scale :                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ           (0-19)/100 = In a nutshell, it sucked!                           บ
 บ          (20-39)/100 = Still crap but slightly better.                     บ
 บ          (40-49)/100 = Possibly worth downloading.                         บ
 บ          (50-69)/100 = Pretty decent game. Might want to check it out.     บ
 บ          (70-79)/100 = Worth the download if you like that type.           บ
 บ          (80-89)/100 = Very good, 9 outta 10 its worth the download.       บ
 บ          (90-99)/100 = Excellent game, a MUST download.                    บ
 บ              100/100 = HOLY SHIT I'VE NEVER SEEN A BETTER GAME!            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RATINGS are based on the game idea, graphics, sound, playability,     บ
 บ  ingenuity, versatility, and a lot of other words ending in 'ity.'  These  บ
 บ  games are based on what happens on MY COMPUTER ONLY, unless stated        บ
 บ  otherwise.  I always first follow NFO directions, and if those don't      บ
 บ  work or are not available, I then try other ways.  So just b/c it         บ
 บ  doesn't work for me, doesn't mean it won't work for you.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ   iMMORAL CUMBAT (c) 3D XXX REALiTY [01/04]                                บ
 บ                                                       บ
 บ         ฒ   ฒ                                บ
 บ   ฒ        ฿฿฿ ฿ ฿฿                                 บ
 บ    ฐฐ      ฐฐฐฐ ฐฐ  ฐฐฐ                                 บ
 บ                                                       บ
 บ     ฐฐ      ฐฐ                                      บ
 บ  ฐ          ฐฐ ฐ                                บ
 บ     ฒ฿    ฒ  ฒ                                    บ
 บ      ฿฿       ฿฿    ฿฿ tZ!                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       IMMORAL CUMBAT iS A FANTASY ADULT                                    บ
 บ       ADVENTURE GAME. ENJOY THE QUALiTY!                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      If you haven't played the older versions of this classically bad      บ
 บ  game, then you should check it out for a laugh.  It's a first person 3D   บ
 บ  perspective (Doom like) in black and white, except your a dick and you    บ
 บ  shoot cum.  You hit the fire button the hand starts wacking off and then  บ
 บ  it shoots cum.  The game gets boring quick, and the graphics are pretty   บ
 บ  dull.  You shoot at other dicks, old fart 3 inchers, and tits and         บ
 บ  ovaries.  Your life stamina is shown by the length of your dick and       บ
 บ  armor in this game is a condom.  I didn't notice any differences from     บ
 บ  this version and older versions, but supposively they are there.  If you  บ
 บ  want a good laugh, go ahead, if not dont bother.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RATING : 28/100                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Demented Dimensions BBS                                                   บ
 บ      Brings You                                                            บ
 บ    Shattered Steel                                                         บ
 บ  Interactive Preview CD                                                    บ
 บ       [01/08]                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Yes, I do occasionally review demos, and this is one of those times.  บ
 บ  This is a playable preview of this upcoming Mechwarrior like game.  In    บ
 บ  fact, it's pretty much exactly like Mechwarrior.  Nice graphics, and      บ
 บ  layout for a demo, with pretty much all the options.  If you want to see  บ
 บ  what it's like so when the full version comes out you can see if it'll    บ
 บ  be worth the download, I reccomend getting it.  If you liked Mechwarrior  บ
 บ  you should also get this.  You will need at least a Pentium 90 to play    บ
 บ  this one.  You basically, like in MW, just go around and shoot at other   บ
 บ  robot like fighting machines, you have missions to follow, etc.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RATING : 52/100                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  Note : Demo was released and then a day later the full was out.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RPG, with lots of interaction and boring non-humorous talking         บ
 บ  between characters.  The movement (with the mouse) is kind of a pain to   บ
 บ  manipulate and to do actions, but you manage.  Music is gay, no           บ
 บ  noticeable sfx.  It's the usual plot of your space ship landing on some   บ
 บ  strange land inhabited by other cretures/people.  Game gets boring        บ
 บ  quick.  You have an eagle's eye view over the land and people.  Not much  บ
 บ  to say, not so hot, don't know why Reflux thought it was the best game    บ
 บ  this year, because it's not.  If you like RPGs with lots of talking and   บ
 บ  roaming around not so hot graphic areas, then you might like this, but    บ
 บ  even then, you might not.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RATING : 40/100 (demo)                                                บ
 บ      RATING : 42/100 (full)                                                บ

 บ      This is a DEMO.  However, no one said shit to me about it being one.  บ
 บ  Nothing in the nfo about it either.  This is a playable demo though, and  บ
 บ  I guess I can talk about it briefly, before I give it the phat O.         บ
 บ  Basically, you've got 3 choices of vehicles, and after that it's          บ
 บ  Terminal Velocity in a car.  Well, not as good as TV, but you get the     บ
 บ  idea.                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      :HAVOC:>  <--- SlAp M3 s0m3 0f dAt pLuS OH!                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Monster Truck Madness Beta 2 [01/21]                                      บ
 บ     ____      _________ ________                                           บ
 บ    ||  #|____||       #||      #\                                          บ
 บ    ||   |    ||   |    ||   |    |                                         บ
 บ    |:        |:   |    |:   |    |Cr                                       บ
 บ  ..|_______  |\______  |______  /....                                      บ
 บ  :::::::๘___/:::::๘___/::::๘___/:::::                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Not bad.  It's definitely a beta, still swaps and pauses right in     บ
 บ  the middle of gameplay, along with a couple audio glitches thrown in for  บ
 บ  good measure, and it installed its own directX2 drivers without asking    บ
 บ  (quite unlike MS).  I'll like it a lot better once the final comes out.   บ
 บ  I do have to say that the synth muzak flippin rocks though and the        บ
 บ  grafix are a lot better than average.  This will probably be one of       บ
 บ  those "unbelievable directX games" I talked about a couple weeks ago.     บ
 บ  As far as the juice of the game, you can pick one out of about 10 of the  บ
 บ  most popular monster trucks to race with.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There are 4 different types of races too.  Drag (side by side car     บ
 บ  crush), Rally (offroad enduro type), Circuit, and Tournament.  You can    บ
 บ  set up suspension, gearbox, and tires on your truck for the different     บ
 บ  types of tracks/races.  Don't have more than 4 other trucks racing        บ
 บ  against you when you first start out though, the traffic kinda sucks.     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There are many different resolutions, textures, and toggles to        บ
 บ  optimize video/processor speed, as well as audio, and joy/keybd setup.    บ
 บ  As a little side note, from what I gather about the help files included,  บ
 บ  MS is planning on devoting a whole webpage to this game, with possible    บ
 บ  tournament type netgames once the game goes final.  This one will         บ
 บ  definitely be worth checking out!                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      POINTS : 74 - I took some points off because it's a beta and has a    บ
 บ                    couple problems.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ GAME REVIEWS, RATINGS, UN-BIASED OPINIONS, HELP/TIPS FOR INSTALLING GAMES! บ
 บ [][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][] บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Rating scale :                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ           (0-19)/100 = In a nutshell, it sucked!                           บ
 บ          (20-39)/100 = Still crap but slightly better.                     บ
 บ          (40-49)/100 = Possibly worth downloading.                         บ
 บ          (50-69)/100 = Pretty decent game. Might want to check it out.     บ
 บ          (70-79)/100 = Worth the download if you like that type.           บ
 บ          (80-89)/100 = Very good, 9 outta 10 its worth the download.       บ
 บ          (90-99)/100 = Excellent game, a MUST download.                    บ
 บ              100/100 = HOLY SHIT I'VE NEVER SEEN A BETTER GAME!            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RATINGS are based on the game idea, graphics, sound, playability,     บ
 บ  ingenuity, versatility, and a lot of other words ending in 'ity.'  These  บ
 บ  games are based on what happens on MY COMPUTER ONLY, unless stated        บ
 บ  otherwise.  I always first follow NFO directions, and if those don't      บ
 บ  work or are not available, I then try other ways.  So just b/c it         บ
 บ  doesn't work for me, doesn't mean it won't work for you.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  =======\___/===๙1911๙CD๙DIVISION๙======\___/                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      "Holy Cow" -Phil Rizuto.  Yes, Holy Cow, holy pigs, and HOLY SHIT.    บ
 บ  Man, this game is sweet as sugar.  It's by far the best baseball game     บ
 บ  out, and for those who like arcade type baseball games, rather than the   บ
 บ  sim, this one is the best ever.  This game has it all as do many          บ
 บ  baseball games.  The game play is quick, to the point, and has great      บ
 บ  sound effects and announcer (yes it really has an announcer in the 45     บ
 บ  disks, no addons).  The announcer also doesn't just say lame ass like     บ
 บ  "Now batting 1st baseman."  No sir, he says the name of the player,       บ
 บ  sometimes comments if he has scored a run and stuff like that.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Anyone with at least a 486 can run this game, because it has a nice   บ
 บ  low resolution mode, that at first may seem crappy, but you'll soon see   บ
 บ  it ain't that bad.  Those of you with Pentium 75+ will be able to         บ
 บ  experience the beautiful high resolution graphics that make this game     บ
 บ  even more exciting to play.  It even has modem play and serial play.      บ
 บ  Home run derby of course, season of course, and all of the types of play  บ
 บ  you could think of.  Real players, real teams, and real stats.  This is   บ
 บ  as close as we've gotten to a really good baseball game that was          บ
 บ  actually a GAME and not so statistical.  It's not impossible to hit the   บ
 บ  ball, and the game follows no "boring nintendo like" patterns where you   บ
 บ  can always steal or stuff like that (I've actually even been able to      บ
 บ  pick off the computer from first base, when it had a big lead).           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This game is without a doubt, a must for anyone looking for sports    บ
 บ  or baseball games, and a definite worth checking out for others, unless   บ
 บ  you despise sports.  Easy to install, no subst, it's what we here in      บ
 บ  `Reviewland' wish everything was like.  So go grab your mit, your bat,    บ
 บ  and oh, bring your balls <G>.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RATING : 91/100                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ   The Civil War (c) Empire Interactive [1/7]                               บ

 บ  =======\___/===๙1911๙CD๙DIVISION๙======\___/                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This is one of the lesser quality war games.  It's a simple map of    บ
 บ  the flags and they move towards each other and you get to have the fun    บ
 บ  of controlling the supplies and people, etc.  This one ain't too hot,     บ
 บ  lot's of different settings inside the game, but it's pretty plain and    บ
 บ  basic looking.  Sound like went off after the opening for some reason.    บ
 บ  Looks pretty boring, if you find yourself playing this for more than 5    บ
 บ  minutes on a friday or saturday night, call 1-800-DR-KEVORKIAN and ask    บ
 บ  about the special "Fast Serve" plan.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RATING : 37/100                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  TOTAL MELTDOWN (c) Sierra            [01/48]                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Bad BAD BAD Prestige!  Naughty naughty!  Yuck, this is not only       บ
 บ  freeware, but it is crap too (oh wait those are the same thing).  This    บ
 บ  is a collection of addon shit for Duke Nukem 3D.  It's got shitload of    บ
 บ  .maps, most of which were already released in Nuke It and other misc.     บ
 บ  packagings.  It include's an install which doesn't work and stuff, and a  บ
 บ  shitty program to view levels, which sucks balls anyway.  This is just a  บ
 บ  plain out waste of time.  It includes also some animations, but it tells  บ
 บ  you nothing about how to run it, and there is just so much crap in this,  บ
 บ  that it takes up like 170 megs, (even though when I deleted it, I had     บ
 บ  333 more megs) and it's a total waste of space and time to download.      บ
 บ  Even if you're a die hard Duke Nukem 3D fan, don't waste your precious    บ
 บ  life.                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RATING : 26/100                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  =======\___/===๙1911๙CD๙DIVISION๙======\___/                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This review brought to you by the letter C, K, and a close friend of  บ
 บ  Z, Mr. Y.  This game closely compares to C&C, but it just lacks the       บ
 บ  faster paced action that C&C has.  The game, although could easily made   บ
 บ  better by some faster movement of the characters (and it has nothing to   บ
 บ  do with the CPU, they are just designed to move only a certain amount of  บ
 บ  space per time) and maybe a little more close up action.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The game has two people, you and the computer, and your job is to     บ
 บ  take over sections of the land and build up an army, get weapons and      บ
 บ  vehicles etc.  Once you've done so (or you could just go straight for     บ
 บ  it) you try to knock down the enemies fort.  Also, the movement of the    บ
 บ  map is pretty damn slow too, and the controlling of it is a pain in the   บ
 บ  ass when you have people all over the map and you are trying to move      บ
 บ  them a little further down past where the screen shows (you can use the   บ
 บ  zoomed out map, but it's still a pain in the ass).                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Plus, every time you click on one of your guys it centers the         บ
 บ  screen, pain.  The robots (they are the ones who fight) talk to you on    บ
 บ  videophone and say stuff like "What the hell is wrong with you, I said    บ
 บ  we are under attack."  Sometimes they will give you an attitude, if for   บ
 บ  example, you tried to send one soldier after a huge tank, it will say     บ
 บ  "Are you crazy?" or "No way!" but it will still of course do it.  The     บ
 บ  game could be a lot better if they just made it more fast paced.  But if  บ
 บ  you don't mind waiting 1-2 mins for your guy to go from your side to the  บ
 บ  other, then by all means, try this one out.  It certainly isn't on the    บ
 บ  C&C level, but it tries to be.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RATING : 60/100                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    TIME COMMANDO (C) ADELINE/EA/ACTIVISION [01/45]                         บ
 บ           ฿ ฿฿   ๚                              บ
 บ   ฿       ฐ       ฐ                         บ
 บ          ฿                                 บ
 บ     ฿      ฒ   ฿฿฿   ฐฐฐ                       บ
 บ        ฐฐ  ฿฿  ฒ฿฿ฒ                            บ
 บ   ฿฿฿฿฿    ฿฿฿฿฿ ฿  ฿฿฿       ฿฿฿                         บ
 บ  ฿฿     r  e  f  l  u  x  !      ฐฐ         ฿฿                       บ
 บ   ฿    ฤฤฤฤฤฤ ฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤ-- - -ฤ -ฤฤฤ-ฤ                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Wow, I was impressed by the looks of this game.  Although it's more   บ
 บ  fighting than it was using your brain, it's still a good game.  How can   บ
 บ  you describe this one, well, picture it this way, you know how in Alone   บ
 บ  in the Dark you could fight, well that's what this game is like, except   บ
 บ  it's on a better game engine, better fighting, and better graphics.       บ
 บ  This game amazed me because it runs smoothly on anything (486+) in the    บ
 บ  top notch gfx mode.  It's really fun to play, but there are only a few    บ
 บ  levels because of the large size.  Also don't use the Reflux installer,   บ
 บ  I think it's set for *.r* and so it goes in a loop, do it manually.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      This game is one worth checking out if you like those 3D looking      บ
 บ  games and wish they had more action to it.  Although the game gets        บ
 บ  boring, it's still a nice step in technology and looks cool to show off   บ
 บ  to people.  There was also an animation pack, which will get it's review  บ
 บ  in next issue.  Great game, but lacks the umph (more levels) that the CD  บ
 บ  would have.  Also, once I got to the level "European Middle Age - Level   บ
 บ  1" I would keep on beating it and it would just take me back to that,     บ
 บ  seems like the ending is not there or there is none.  Here are two        บ
 บ  passwords, apparently the only ones you can get from playing this rip:    บ
 บ  VSINSYEA and TWXPPGGA or RDDXBPGA.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RATING : 77/100                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  minutes of my time though, which is about 10 more than I thought it       บ
 บ  would.  The game is almost exactly like tetris, as far as the shit        บ
 บ  dropping out the top goes, but it drops animals and food instead of       บ
 บ  shapes.  Only certain animals eat certain food and the more food they     บ
 บ  eat the more points you get.  Kinda hard to explain, so either screw it,  บ
 บ  or leech it to find out.  The grafix were a little better than average    บ
 บ  for a game like this, and the midis were cool too.  2 player mode was     บ
 บ  also included, like side by side Dr. Mario.  Be sure to get the .dll      บ
 บ  fixpak for this too.                                                      บ

 บ  =======\___/===1911CDDIVISION======\___/                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Another SimXXXX type of game, but I like this one for some reason.    บ
 บ  Maybe because there's combat stuff in it too?  Maybe because there's a    บ
 บ  different type of strategy involved?  Dunno.  There's definitely a lot    บ
 บ  of stuff to do (and for me, to fuck up..heh).  The main goal in this is   บ
 บ  to build up your technologies, while keeping your people fed and happy,   บ
 บ  not running out of resources, and not getting waxed by your competitors.  บ
 บ  I picked a crappy race when I started, and my competitors got a lot more  บ
 บ  colonists than I did.  Ya gotta have a lot of colonists for a fast        บ
 บ  growing empire.  I had a little trouble trying to do stuff, but a nice    บ
 บ  help system wasn't ripped in case you can't figure out how to do          บ
 บ  something.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The music is pretty cool, the graphics are about like any other       บ
 บ  SimXXX game, and netplay wasn't ripped either.  A little side note,       บ
 บ  Ionizer couldn't get this to work on his Win31 box, it says it will       บ
 บ  under Win32s in the nfo, so I dunno if the nfo is correct on that.  No    บ
 บ  problems installing it in 95 tho, just run Razor's supah hax0red          บ
 บ  Setup.exe.  WinG and the Adobe .pdf reader were included too.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      All in all, I can pretty much say that this game seems to be SimCity  บ
 บ  taken to a new and interesting level.  Nice game, from someone who barfs  บ
 บ  at the word SimShitty.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Ionizer's Note : NFO said it would run in Win3.1, but it didn't.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
