 บ   Mission Force: CyberStorm (c) SSI [1/24]                                 บ
 บ  _____ _____  ____ _____  ________________                                 บ
 บ  \_   | \   \/   / _   /__\_   \_/   _    \                                บ
 บ   |   _  \_  \ _/  \   \ __/___/ |   /    /                                บ
 บ   |___|   |____|___/   /_\   \___|_______/                                 บ
 บ    ::d|___|::::::.\___/.:.\___\::::::::::                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Sure it's 24 disks... if you got a leet ass 2.88 floppy drive.  So in     บ
 บ  order to install this and keep the zips, you'll need 373 megz.  Yeah,     บ
 บ  yeah, so it's under the 50 disk limit, big deal.  Doesn't mean that it    บ
 บ  doesn't suck.  Actually, the game itself wasn't entirely too awful, but   บ
 บ  it was a really shitty rip and not worth the download time.  You can't    บ
 บ  see any of the mission briefings (to tell you what kind of equipment you  บ
 บ  need), or any of the debriefings (where they tell you how god-like you    บ
 บ  are when you wax all the bad guys).  This isn't one of those 1st person   บ
 บ  3d mech games either, it's one of those 3rd person, hex style maps where  บ
 บ  you have to move a guy here, move a guy there, shoot here, shoot there,   บ
 บ  and end turn so the bad guy can move.  Of course, would you expect        บ
 บ  anything different from SSI?                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The pre-mission command center was way cooler than all the            บ
 บ  in-mission graphics.  When it first loaded up and I saw the command       บ
 บ  center stuff, I thought, "Hey wow, fuck, this is cool shit!"  Until the   บ
 บ  actual mission started, when I thought, "I spent HOW MUCH time leeching   บ
 บ  this?"  Kinda reminds me of any of the 1000 scrolly shootemups for the    บ
 บ  PSX.  All the intro, config, and pre-game stuff rocks, but the game       บ
 บ  sucks.  Oh well, this thing wasn't a very rewarding experience, due to    บ
 บ  the ripping of all the text.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      POINTS : 48 - Not worth the time/space.  Hybrid, release the          บ
 บ                    brief/debrief stuff and I might change that score.      บ
 บ                    Better yet, fix that 148 mb file, and repackage it      บ
 บ                    smaller with the text stuff.                            บ

 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 06/06/96 -> 06/19/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

                                         ฿     r e v i e w s !

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 06/20/96 -> 07/03/96            ณ  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 07/04/96 -> 07/17/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 07/18/96 -> 07/31/96            ณ  บ

 บ    Author  : Pawn                                                          บ
 บ    Subject : Explosives : Muric Acid Bomb                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, this is my first of hopefuly many articles that I will be       บ
 บ  writing for RCN!  So if this kinda starts to suck just stay with me       บ
 บ  because I will try to do my best explaning how to make many explosives    บ
 บ  of destruction.  Anyway, let's get on to the good stuff!  This bomb was   บ
 บ  orignated by me, Pawn, so I should be able to explain this pretty well.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Materials                                                             บ
 บ      ---------                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       2-Liter Bottle (Like a Coke Bottle)                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Aluminum Foil                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Squirt Bottle (Not Required)                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Muric Acid (Muric or Hydrocloric Acid)                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  1.) After you have all the materials, take the a 1 foot by 1 foot piece   บ
 บ      of foil and start ripping it into 1/2 to 3/4 by 2 or 3 inch peices.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                            ____                                            บ
 บ                           |    |                                           บ
 บ                           |    |                                           บ
 บ                           |    | <-- 2 to 3 inches                         บ
 บ                           |    |                                           บ
 บ                           |____|                                           บ
 บ                             ^                                              บ
 บ                              \ 1/2 to 3/4 inch                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  2.) Then, making sure that all the pieces are done, slide them all into   บ
 บ      the the 2-liter bottle, try not to crumple them up.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  3.) Pour about 1/2 of a cup of the muric acid into the squirt bottle.     บ
 บ      Get one of the squirt bottles that have one of those squirt caps so   บ
 บ      you can get squirt the acid out fast.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  4.) Lastly, take the squirt bottle and the 2-liter bottle with the        บ
 บ      aluminum foil in it to the place where you want to let it off and     บ
 บ      squirt all the acid into the 2-liter bottle as fast as you can and    บ
 บ      then put the cap on and throw it!  You might want to watch it from a  บ
 บ      distance because when this thing goes off, it is big and load!        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

                       ฿ h a c k e r z   c o r n e r !

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Coolzie                                                       บ
 บ    Subject : 4240-419-001-340 (Invalid)                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Most of the following information came from a lot of sources, so      บ
 บ  they may look redundant to some of the more knowledgable individuals,     บ
 บ  but I felt that a few people may be interested in reading this.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Obtaining a Credit Card Number                                            บ
 บ  ------------------------------                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There are many ways to obtain the information needed to card          บ
 บ  something.  The most important things needed are the card number and the  บ
 บ  expiration date.  Having the card-holder's name doesn't hurt, but it is   บ
 บ  not essential.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      One way to obtain all the information needed is by trashing.  The     บ
 บ  way this is done is simple.  You walk around your area or any other area  บ
 บ  and find a store, mall, supermarket, etc., that throws their garbage      บ
 บ  outside on the sidewalk or dumpster.  Rip the bag open and see if you     บ
 บ  can find any carbons at all.  If you find little shreds of credit card    บ
 บ  carbons, then it is most likely not worth your time to tape together.     บ
 บ  Find a store that does not rip their carbons at all or only in half.      บ
 บ  General rule when trashing is to dress like a bum.  If you are a bum,     บ
 บ  dress normally.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Another way is to bullshit the number out of someone.  That is call   บ
 บ  them up and say "Hello, this is Visa security and we have a report that   บ
 บ  your card was stolen."  They will deny it and you will try to get it out  บ
 บ  of them from that point on.  You could say, "It wasn't stolen?  Well      บ
 บ  what is the expiration date and maybe we can fix the problem.  Ok... and  บ
 บ  what is the number on your card, sir?  Thank you very much and have a     บ
 บ  nice day."  Or think of something to that degree.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Another way to get card numbers is through systems such as TRW and    บ
 บ  CBI, this is the hard way, and probably not worth the trouble unless you  บ
 บ  are an expert on the system.  Using credit card numbers posted on BBSes   บ
 บ  is risky.  The only advantage is that there is a good chance that other   บ
 บ  people will use it, thus decreasing the chances of being the              บ
 บ  sole-offender.  The last method of getting numbers is very good also.     บ
 บ  In most video rental stores, they take down your credit card number when  บ
 บ  you join to back-up your rentals.  So if you could manage to steal the    บ
 บ  list or make a copy of it, then you are set for a LONG time.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      More modern methods include taking advantage of online services and   บ
 บ  Internet shopping malls.  I will not go into details about this, you'll   บ
 บ  have to figure this out yourself.  To give you an idea how easy this      บ
 บ  could be, take for example America Online.  They have 6 million           บ
 บ  subscribers.  A rather large percentage of that number consist of         บ
 บ  idiots, morons or dumbasses and I personally have "fished" at least 100k  บ
 บ  on some nights and acquired at least 5,000 full info CCs.  Don't ask      บ
 บ  how, that's my style.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Basically, all you have to do is pull some very skillful hi-tech      บ
 บ  bullshitting.  You pretend to be staff/sysop and tell the victim that     บ
 บ  there are problems or whatever you can think of.  Outside the scope of    บ
 บ  carding, you can also use this method to obtain passwords to accounts.    บ
 บ  Needless to say, card a fake account first.  By the way, do not look for  บ
 บ  me in the private chatroom CARDING.  I don't go there.  All I saw were    บ
 บ  whimps who couldn't do the carding themselves, and a few smart people     บ
 บ  who took advantage of this.  I think I saw this published in the last     บ
 บ  issue of RCN, and unfortunately, I have met some who fell prey to this    บ
 บ  trick.  What can I say?  You deserve it.  Blah...                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Sometimes, some establishments will accept any card number as long    บ
 บ  as it is valid.  The algorithms for computing credit card numbers are     บ
 บ  public information.  Hey, I've coded my own program to do this in my      บ
 บ  spare time, it's not difficult.  You can read it from the alt.2600 FAQ    บ
 บ  and probably find it implemented on several programs, most notable is     บ
 บ  Credit Master.  Generally, generated numbers don't work, but sometimes    บ
 บ  you can find certain bank index numbers which do.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      For example, using a generated number of the prefix 4921-85 can get   บ
 บ  you access to most online services.  Yeah, you porn lovers can subscribe  บ
 บ  or call stuff.  You can even use some of these to card phone calls (i.e.  บ
 บ  1-800-CALL-ATT).  Use a payphone.  I love their advertisement, "Know the  บ
 บ  code,"  Muhahhahaha.  Go recharge some prepaid phone cards.  Get them     บ
 บ  everywhere.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Choosing a Victim                                                         บ
 บ  -----------------                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Once you have the card number, it is time to make the order.  The     บ
 บ  type of places that are easiest to victimize are small businesses that    บ
 บ  do mail order or even local stores that deliver.  If you have an ad for   บ
 บ  a place with something you want and the order number is NOT a 1-800       บ
 บ  number, then chances are better that you will succeed.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      When you call the place up to make the order, you must have several   บ
 บ  things readily at hand.  These are the things you will need, a name,      บ
 บ  telephone number, business phone, card number (4 digit bank code if the   บ
 บ  card is MasterCard), expiration date, and a complete shipping and         บ
 บ  billing address.  I will talk about all of these in detail.  A personal   บ
 บ  tip, when I call to make an order, it usually goes much smoother if the   บ
 บ  person I am talking to is a woman.  In many cases they are more gullible  บ
 บ  than men.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A name, you could use the name on the card or the name of the person  บ
 บ  who you are going to send the merchandise to.  Or you could use the name  บ
 บ  on the card and have it shipped to the person who lives at the drop (say  บ
 บ  it is a gift or something).  The name is really not that important        บ
 บ  because when the company verifies the card, the person's name is never    บ
 บ  mentioned, EXCEPT when you have a Preffered Visa card.  Then the name is  บ
 บ  mentioned.  You can tell if you have a Preffered Visa card by the PV to   บ
 บ  the right of the expiration date on the carbon.  Now, phone all day long  บ
 บ  waiting for the company to call (which they will), then the phone number  บ
 บ  to give them as your home-phone could be one of the following, a number   บ
 บ  that is ALWAYS busy, a number that ALWAYS rings, a payphone number, low   บ
 บ  end of a loop (and you will wait on the other end), or a popular BBS.     บ
 บ  NEVER give them your home phone because they will find out as soon as     บ
 บ  their investigations start and they check who the phone belongs to.  The  บ
 บ  best thing would be to have a payphone call forward your house.  If you   บ
 บ  can beige-box a neighbor's and connect to it remotely, that would be      บ
 บ  even better.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The card number, the cards you will use will be Visa, MasterCard,     บ
 บ  American Express, and Discover.  The best is by far Visa.  It is the      บ
 บ  most straight-forward.  MasterCard is pretty cool except for the bank     บ
 บ  code.  When they ask for the bank code, they sometimes also ask for the   บ
 บ  bank that issued it.  When they ask that, just say the biggest bank you   บ
 บ  know of in your area.  Try to avoid American Express.  They tend to lead  บ
 บ  full scale investigations.  Unfortunately, American Express is the most   บ
 บ  popular card out.  When telling the person who is taking your call the    บ
 บ  card number, say it slowly, clearly, and with confidence.  For example,   บ
 บ  if the card number is 5396-1234-5678-9012, pause after each set of fours  บ
 บ  so you don't have to repeat yourself.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The date of the expiration date must be at LEAST in that month.  It   บ
 บ  is best with more than three months to go.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The address is more commonly referred to as the 'drop.'  Well, the    บ
 บ  drop can range from an abandoned building to your next door neighbor's    บ
 บ  apartment.  If you plan to send it to an apartment building, then be      บ
 บ  sure NOT to include an apartment number.  This will confuse UPS or the    บ
 บ  postage men a little and they will leave the package in the lobby.  Here  บ
 บ  is a list of various drops - the house next door whose family is on       บ
 บ  vacation, the apartment that was just moved out of, the old church that   บ
 บ  will be knocked down in six months, your friend's house who has           บ
 บ  absolutely nothing to do with the type of merchandise you will buy and    บ
 บ  who will also not crack under heat from Feds, etc.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There are also services that hold merchandise for you, but            บ
 บ  personally, I would not trust them.  And forget about P.O. Boxes because  บ
 บ  you need ID to get one and most places don't ship to them anyway.  If     บ
 บ  you work for a company or have a large group that has an account on       บ
 บ  something like Mailboxes Etc, that might work.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Other aspects of carding include verifying cards, seeing if they      บ
 บ  were reported stolen.  Stores need to verify credit cards when someone    บ
 บ  purchases something with one.  They call up a service that checks to see  บ
 บ  if the customer has the money in the bank.  The merchant identifies       บ
 บ  himself with a merchant number.  The service then holds the money that    บ
 บ  the merchant verified on reserve.  When the merchant sends in the credit  บ
 บ  card form, the service sends the merchant the money.  The service holds   บ
 บ  the money for three days and if no form appears then it is put back into  บ
 บ  the bank.  The point is that if you want to verify something then you     บ
 บ  should verify it for a little amount and odds are that there will be      บ
 บ  more in the bank.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The good thing about verification is that if the card doesn't exist   บ
 บ  or if it is stolen, then the service will tell you.  To verify            บ
 บ  MasterCard and Visa, try the following number.  It is voice :             บ
 บ  1-800-327-1111, the merchant code is 596719.  Whoa, this information is   บ
 บ  old, you may need to get a more recent one.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Stolen cards, MasterCard and Visa come out with a small catalog       บ
 บ  every week where they publish EVERY stolen or fraudulantly used card.  I  บ
 บ  get this every week by trashing the same place on the same day.  If you   บ
 บ  ever find it trashing, then try to get it every week.  If you got         บ
 บ  connections in a store, they usually have this.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Identifying cards, Visa card numbers begin with a 4 and have either   บ
 บ  13 or 16 digits.  MasterCard card numbers begin with a 5 and have 16      บ
 บ  digits.  Discover card numbers begin with a 6 and have 16 digits.         บ
 บ  American Express begins with a 3 and has 15 digits.  They all have the    บ
 บ  following formats :                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3xxx-xxxxxx-xxxxx   American Express / Diner's Club                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      4xxx-xxx-xxx-xxx    Visa                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      4xxx-xxxx-xxxx-xxxx Visa                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      5xxx-xxxx-xxxx-xxxx MasterCard                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      6xxx-xxxx-xxxx-xxxx Discover                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A gold card simply means that credit is good for $5000.  Without a    บ
 บ  gold card, credit would normally be $2000 or less.  To recognize a gold   บ
 บ  card on a carbon, there are several techniques :                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      American Express- None.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Visa            - PV instead of CV.  Note, you must have the          บ
 บ                        cardholder's name to verify a PV.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      MasterCard      - An asterix can signify a gold card, but this        บ
 บ                        changes depending when the card was issued.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      THe following is a dialog between a carder and the phone operator to  บ
 บ  help you get the idea :                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Operator> American Computer Goods, may I help you?                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Carder> Hi, I would like to place an order please.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Operator> Sure, what would you like to order?                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Carder> 20 zip disks and a 1 gigabyte drive.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Operator> Ok, is there anything else?                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Carder>  No thank you, that's all for today.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Operator> Ok, how would you like to pay for this?  MasterCard or Visa?   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Carder> Visa.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Operator> And your name is?                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Carder> Justin M. Kalina. (Name on card)                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Operator> And your Visa card number is?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Carder> 4240-419-001-340 (Invalid card)                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Operator> Expiration date?                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Carder> 08-96.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Operator> And where would you like the package shipped to?               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Carder> 49 Shongum Road, Randolph, NJ 07869.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Operator> And what is your home telephone number?                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Carder> 201/328-8405 (This number is actually usually busy)              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Operator> I will also need your business phone number in case we have    บ
 บ             to reach you.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Carder> You can reach me at the same number. 201/328-8405                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Operator> Ok, thank you very much and have nice day.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Carder> Excuse me, when will the package arrive?                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Operator> In 6 to 7 days via UPS.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Carder> Thanks a lot, and have a pleasant day.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now, you wait 6-7 days when the package will arrive at the address    บ
 บ  which is really an abandoned house.  There will be a note on the door     บ
 บ  saying - Hello UPS, please leave all packages for Justin Kalina in the    บ
 บ  lobby or porch.  Thanks a lot, Justin Kalina.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There are a lot of things to card.  Almost every establishment I      บ
 บ  know accepts credit cards.  Although, if you study this carefully, we     บ
 บ  can understand why 2600 or RCN probably believes in the motto : In God    บ
 บ  we trust, all others pay in cash.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      What do you do with the goods?  Use them, sell them, whatever.  If    บ
 บ  you get caught, tough, that's your problem.  I personally have my boys    บ
 บ  do the job for me.  I run my own little ring of carders.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Recognizing Credit Cards                                                  บ
 บ  ------------------------                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       [Sample: American Express]                                           บ
 บ        XXXX XXXXXX XXXXX                                                   บ
 บ        MM/Y1 THRU MM/Y2       Y1                                           บ
 บ        John Doe               AX                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The first date is the date the person got the card, the second date   บ
 บ  is the expriation date, after the expiration date is the same digits in   บ
 บ  the first year.  The American Express Gold has many more numbers (I       บ
 บ  think 6 8 then 8).  If you do find a Gold card keep it for it has a       บ
 บ  $5000.00 backup even when the guy has no money!                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       [Sample: MasterCard]                                                 บ
 บ        5XXX XXXX XXXX XXXX                                                 บ
 บ        XXXX AAA DD-MM-YY MM/YY                                             บ
 บ        John Doe                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The format varies, I have never seen a card that did not start with   บ
 บ  a 5XXX.  There are another 4 digits on the next line that is sometimes    บ
 บ  asked for when ordering stuff, (and rarely a 3 digit letter combo.  The   บ
 บ  first date is the date the person got the card and the second date is     บ
 บ  the expiration date.  Master ard is almost always accepted at stores.     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       [Sample: Visa]                                                       บ
 บ        XXXX XXX(X) XXX(X) XXX(X)                                           บ
 บ        MM/YY    MM/YY*Visa                                                 บ
 บ        John Doe                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Visa is the most straight forward of the cards, for it has the name   บ
 บ  right on the card itself, again the first date is the date he got the     บ
 บ  card and the second is the expiration date.  Sometimes the first date is  บ
 บ  left out.  The numbers can either be 4 3 3 3 or 4 4 4 4.  Visa is also    บ
 บ  almost always accepted at stores, therefore, the best of cards to use.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      My personal experience includes carding modems, books, flowers,       บ
 บ  Internet accounts, protein skimmers (aquarium stuff), ink cartridges,     บ
 บ  software (hey you suppliers check this out, card your warez), t-shirts,   บ
 บ  international phone calls, music CDs, VHS tapes (UFC and Beavis and       บ
 บ  Butthead), mice, keyboards, speakers, sound systems.  Blah.. I forget     บ
 บ  what else I've gotten.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Most of the time now, I just have someone else do it.  They are       บ
 บ  usually loyal, and sometimes I just do a special arrangement for the      บ
 บ  more experienced ones.  I don't do stuff over $2,000 worth, so I can      บ
 บ  honestly tell you that I've never tried carding a laptop.  If you have    บ
 บ  to sign for a package, use your own pen, and sign a fake name or          บ
 บ  whoever.  Sometimes, leaving a $1 tip on the door stuck to your note      บ
 บ  helps.  Sometimes, knowing the delivery mailman can be beneficial.        บ
 บ  Sometimes, it's not what you know, or what you can do, but who you know.  บ
 บ  Having politicians in your pocket, connections with gangs, tie-ups with   บ
 บ  store establishments, or friends in the Mafia (or Yakuza) can do          บ
 บ  wonders.                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I'd say hacking, phreaking, carding, warez and general anarchy are    บ
 บ  woven in the same web.  Some may say carding is a bit on the darker side  บ
 บ  of things.  Then again, that's only my opinion.  Here I am typing away,   บ
 บ  but after this, I am going to go out and play in my sports country club   บ
 บ  field with my carded soccer ball, wearing my carded socks, go skating on  บ
 บ  my carded in-line skates, and look cool in my carded shades.  Too bad my  บ
 บ  car had to be stolen, you can't have everything.  I'm just kidding about  บ
 บ  the car.  :)                                                              บ

 บ    Author  : Anonymous                                                     บ
 บ    Subject : Fake Account Generators                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Fake accounts have been made by warez pups throughout the history of  บ
 บ  AOL.  I started making fakes during the AOL v2.5 times.  It was an easy   บ
 บ  way of getting warez without paying that much money.  I had to pay for    บ
 บ  the phone line, that was about it.  At about May/June 1996, AOL started   บ
 บ  catching AOL faake accounts, they verified to see if the credit card      บ
 บ  numbers were real.  This disappointed a lot of people, which led more     บ
 บ  people to make fake account creators that would trick AOL.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Da Chronic made a fake account creator included with his AOHell.      บ
 บ  His fake account creator was the only one to use a checking account.  It  บ
 บ  never worked.  Radiator's AOLSD would have probably worked, but there     บ
 บ  was one problem.  They didn't include a credit card number, so you had    บ
 บ  to get a real one.  The rest of the people probably took AOHell and       บ
 บ  AOLSD, decompiled and made another version of their own.  They never      บ
 บ  modified the code, so the fake account creators still never worked.  By   บ
 บ  the way, if somone does get a VB Decompiler (not DOdis), send it over     บ
 บ  for trade.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      These fake account creators did work.  The UGK fake account creator,  บ
 บ  this was one of the best fake account creators.  It was the first         บ
 บ  working one I got, so I made about 20 fakes.  It was not password         บ
 บ  protected, so the certificate # and passwords were drained quickly.  The  บ
 บ  Magik FAC written by Snoop also worked.  This was a fairly new FAC made   บ
 บ  between the time UGK's died and the AOL crackdown of fake accounts.       บ
 บ  This was password protected so the certificate stuff lasted a while.  It  บ
 บ  wasn't anything like Skitzo's.  You could easily hex Magik, but Skitzo's  บ
 บ  was a password that wasn't even near the question area.  This made it a   บ
 บ  lot harder to crack.  Skitzo's FAC was supposed to work, that was what    บ
 บ  everyone said, but when I tried, it never worked.  It must have been the  บ
 บ  build number which was probably out of date.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Since the AOL crackdown on fake accounts.  Only a few FACs still      บ
 บ  work, one of these was the new Skitzo's FAC.  I heard it's supposed to    บ
 บ  work, but I've never gotten hold of it.  A number of other FACs were      บ
 บ  supposed to work, but I've never tried them nor have I gotten them.       บ
 บ  Since fake accounts are a lot harder to make without using a real credit  บ
 บ  card number, getting Level 8 OverHead accounts was the solution.  Here    บ
 บ  is a piece of mail that was forwarded back and forth :                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Forwarded message:                                                        บ
 บ  Subj:     Your OverHead Account                                           บ
 บ  Date:     96-06-18 04:50:39 EDT                                           บ
 บ  From:     Steve Case                                                      บ
 บ  To:       TOSAdvisor                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Good afternoon, John.  Here is your OverHead account generator.       บ
 บ  This is just the basic Level 8 OverHead generator.  Once you download     บ
 บ  this file, simply unzip it, then run the program, and within 2-3 days,    บ
 บ  AOL will update your account with all the listed abilities :              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.) FREE unlimited time online.                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.) The ability to kick an annoying user from a chat room.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3.) Log a user offline, if he/she has rightfully so violated our      บ
 บ          Terms of Service.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      4.) Terminate a user's account if he/she has rightfully so violated   บ
 บ          our Terms of Service.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      5.) The ability to remain invisible in a chat room to where no one    บ
 บ          can see you're in the room.                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now remember, these are just a few of much more capabilities allowed  บ
 บ  by Level 8 OverHead account status.  So download, unzip, run the          บ
 บ  COW-OH.EXE while signed on and you'll be set.  Also, distribute this as   บ
 บ  you see fit.  Goodbye for now, John.                                      บ

 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ      Welcome to Dear Road Rebel!  This is going to be YOUR column that is  บ
 บ  a cross between Dear Abby and Dave Berry.  The most important part of     บ
 บ  this is YOUR participation.  If you have ever had a question about the    บ
 บ  scene or just a comment, here's the place!  Have you ever wanted to know  บ
 บ  why some people do this or that?  ASK!  I would love to take it to the    บ
 บ  extreme for you and we will be happy to research it!  I hope you have as  บ
 บ  much fun with this as I will!  Remember, this is YOUR column!             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Dear Road Rebel,                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      First, I'd like to commend you and your fellow RCN members on the     บ
 บ  creation of the RCN emag and the RCN web page which are awesome and very  บ
 บ  inspiring to other groups and wannabe groups.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now, to the main topic, DALNet vs. EFNet (I personally don't think    บ
 บ  UnderNet actually fits into the picture here!).  I have been an EFNet     บ
 บ  regular ever since I introduced myself to the IRC world, which was about  บ
 บ  3 to 4 months ago.  I knew about the warez scene because of my 2 years    บ
 บ  BBSing, and then finally running up a $1400 phone bill in two months (a   บ
 บ  very big FUCK you to AT&T), forcing me to terminate long distance         บ
 บ  connections for an extensive period of time.  I had one or two friends    บ
 บ  that I knew who were on IRC all the time but I had no idea about the      บ
 บ  different EFNet, DALNet, etc., server groups.  Only in the past month     บ
 บ  have I traveled these new domains on DALNet, UnderNet and now NewNet,     บ
 บ  and I quite agree with you that DALNet is one of the best places out      บ
 บ  there to go for warez (which have now been banned on DALNet I'm sorry to  บ
 บ  say).  But, I have to disagree with some things you said about DALNet     บ
 บ  last issue (but I'll have to start a new paragraph first).                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I traveled DALNet's extensive and friendly warez channels as soon as  บ
 บ  I found it, and tried to make as many friends as possible, and possibly   บ
 บ  succeeded making friends with 85% of all the people that I chatted with.  บ
 บ  Until last week when I decided to create my own Fserve/Warez/Trade        บ
 บ  channel, disaster!  I went about the right way to set the channel up,     บ
 บ  got a decent Bot in there, registered the channel, and registered my      บ
 บ  bot's nick and my own nick to be auto-opped in that channel.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      "Cool, no problems there, now to go and find warez lovers to join my  บ
 บ  channel and trade their little shorts off!"  I went into multiple warez   บ
 บ  channels on DALNet and started to subtly invite people and their fserves  บ
 บ  to trade in my channel too, some came, some simply said no, or fuck off.  บ
 บ  After a while watching other peoples' attempts at starting IRC channels,  บ
 บ  I saw that mass invites would bring an equal amount of traders and        บ
 บ  lamers (lamers being the ones that try to flood the channel or take it    บ
 บ  over).  I tried this mass invite thingy making sure that I had proper     บ
 บ  flood protection against these attempts.  People joined, then left, more  บ
 บ  people joined then left, channel ops banned me, then tried desperately    บ
 บ  to takeover and flood me and my channel, people /msg'd me obscene         บ
 บ  comments and remarks, but on the other hand, some people said, "Ok, I     บ
 บ  have an fserve, what do I need to do to have it on your channel?"  Or     บ
 บ  they joined the channel, said hi, when others joined, they all chatted    บ
 บ  together and it went on to be like a normal warez channel.  Then my BIG   บ
 บ  mistake, I joined the warez channels with 25+ people in them, and         บ
 บ  started to mass invite people.  The same things happened as when I        บ
 บ  invited smaller channels, only on a MUCH larger scale!  Anyways, I        บ
 บ  eventually got three fserves in my channel and 5 normal people before it  บ
 บ  was time for me to hang up my modem for another time.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I do not think that I will re-create this channel until I have a      บ
 บ  moderate group of people willing to support the channel.  And if anyone   บ
 บ  else plans to do the same as I did, take this letter as a lesson.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As for what you said about no lag, well... I have found that most     บ
 บ  people try to get on servers that have an IP that is not far from         บ
 บ  one-another, if you get on a far away server, it sucks, big time.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      My final word is, DALNet and EFNet are both equally great, for        บ
 บ  chatting and leeching, but if you want to start a warez channel, make     บ
 บ  sure you have a very good reason to, like starting a new group is         บ
 บ  probably the best reason.  I wouldn't bother starting a trade channel on  บ
 บ  EFNet because, quite frankly, they really are not in short supply of      บ
 บ  them!                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Taiji Hide                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  I saw a few splits, but they were right back in like 10 secs.  As for     บ
 บ  warez, I think DALNet banning warez is a mistake and it will kill their   บ
 บ  servers.  BUT.... we will wait and see, all I know right now is that      บ
 บ  DALNet has been around for quite awhile.  BUT it isn't growing up, if     บ

 บ  life.                                                                     บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Aquarius> Don't be defensive if you make a mistake on IRC.  Nobody       บ
 บ             cares.  Stay focused on getting it done right.  Nobody is      บ
 บ             perfect, not even guys from Napalm.  Well, Napalm is a little  บ
 บ             more less perfect than most, but if Napalm can learn, so can   บ
 บ             you!                                                           บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Data                                                          บ
 บ    Subject : Women on the Internet                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Let us take the opposite sex, the female, and why she goes on the     บ
 บ  Internet.  I think this is best told through an experience I had a few    บ
 บ  weeks ago.  As I see it, there are certain aspects to look out for when   บ
 บ  talking to a girl online with any provider, be it IRC, or America         บ
 บ  Online.  Let me tell you a story...                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      One day, I was kinda bored, so I decided to call a BBS down in        บ
 บ  Fremont, California.  I usually try to stay away from that board, but     บ
 บ  sometimes I just go on to be a pain in the ass, or to play some BRE,      บ
 บ  Barren Realms Elite, a BBS door game.  Anyway, I found a girl chatting    บ
 บ  with this guy in a private room.  Now, Fubar is known for its sexual      บ
 บ  connotation.  I thought these two were doing the cyber thing because      บ
 บ  they were both at that age of discovery, and amazement.  The room was     บ
 บ  also private.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I went into the main chatroom, and I started to bug the man in the    บ
 บ  private room.  He never acknowledged me until later.  This was getting    บ
 บ  me bored, so I decided to start to flirt with the girl in the private     บ
 บ  chatroom.  I was doing all of this through private messaging.  The girl,  บ
 บ  right away, got really defensive, and was wondering why I was flirting    บ
 บ  with her.  I really had no reason, and I told her that.  She didn't       บ
 บ  understand that and she continued to put up this fat defense.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now, the guy in the chatroom finally let me in, and as soon as I      บ
 บ  went in, this girl was still questioning me.  I told her again that       บ
 บ  there was no reason.  She still denied what I was saying.  Now, being     บ
 บ  kinda humored by all this, I decided to shoot the shit with her for a     บ
 บ  while.  I was sweet talking her, then the bomb shell hit...               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The girl said, "I bet you are the kinda guy that likes girls for the  บ
 บ  outside, rather than their inside!  Aren't you?!"                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I then said to myself, "Uh oh... I bet she's fat."                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It all added up.  First, she got EXTREMELY defensive about me         บ
 บ  flirting with her.  I think the reason for this is that she does not      บ
 บ  know how to handle being flirted with, and likewise does not know how to  บ
 บ  flirt back.  She thinks she is fat, therefore, she has no self-esteme.    บ
 บ  Second, she started to question my ethics toward dating other females,    บ
 บ  giving comments like, "You only look at the outside beauty rather that    บ
 บ  the inside," or "ALL men are like this!"                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I am not sure if it is because girls have a wanting need to be        บ
 บ  loved, or because they have nothing else to do, but it is, as I see it,   บ
 บ  very sad.  I have learned through my all my girlfriends, and              บ
 บ  acquaintances that girls are very self-conscious about their image, and   บ
 บ  need to feel special.  They need to hear from other people that they are  บ
 บ  'not fat' and that they are 'special.'  It would be fine if girls         บ
 บ  complained like this once in a while, because it is just human nature,    บ
 บ  but they do it CONSTANTLY over the Internet.  I have had experience       บ
 บ  meeting people over the Internet, and in every instance, the girl was     บ
 บ  not to amusing to me.  I usually get bored or pissed because she was      บ
 บ  bitching.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      If people want a relationship, the Internet is NOT the way to get     บ
 บ  baked up.  In my opinion, it would be better to just meet people at a     บ
 บ  local coffee shop, or at a McDonald's.  That way, you can see the person  บ
 บ  that you are meeting, and get to know them while you know what they look  บ
 บ  like.  That way, there are no surprises.  Girls can have the most         บ
 บ  wonderful personality and wit over the Internet, but then if you find     บ
 บ  out that she is fat...                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      ...BOMBS AWAY!!!                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      If any of you are trying to pursue a relationship over the Internet,  บ
 บ  I'd urge you to take my friend's advice.  Either that, or get full body   บ
 บ  photos from the person you're talking to or you just won yourself a new   บ
 บ  platonic friend.  There is a reason why Cindy Crawfords don't hang on     บ
 บ  the Internet.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As for women in the scene, I personally have not gotten my ass        บ
 บ  seriously kicked by a girl while shooting the line on the top sites.  I   บ
 บ  still think that if you're a girl, it shouldn't matter, if you can keep   บ
 บ  up with the elites then you gotta be good.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  Frost                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Digitex                                                       บ
 บ    Subject : I Turned Chicken?!                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I'm now fully convinced that I've become a chicken!  Maybe an elf,    บ
 บ  but I'm not going to bother with the details on that.  But I did go ALL   บ
 บ  the way this time, guys, so fear not, and don't get too excited either.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It all started one day when I was with Mr. Bitching at the Lancaster  บ
 บ  Mall here in Salem, Oregon.  I met his cousin there at the main office    บ
 บ  of Lancaster Mall.  We were about to go to a movie, I think it was        บ
 บ  Twister.  Of course, I hadn't seen it, that's why I decided to go along   บ
 บ  since it's my personal goal to see every high-rated movie that exists on  บ
 บ  this planet.  Well, his cousin struck my attention when I met her, she    บ
 บ  closely resembles Pamela Anderson.  VERY closely resembles her.  Hell,    บ
 บ  if she got some implants, she would BE Pamela Anderson.  Anyway, it       บ
 บ  wasn't until later that anything happened between us.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Where it all started was at her temporary location (more on this      บ
 บ  later) at her grandmother's house.  We were in the old van just talking   บ
 บ  about whatever it is we were talking about, that of which completely      บ
 บ  escapes me at this point.  But I decided then and there that I had a      บ
 บ  certain affection for her, so I had to find some way to get her.  The     บ
 บ  next day, that happened.                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      We were at Mr. Bitching's house and Mr. Bitching was assailing us     บ
 บ  with many rubber bands.  He was armed with a handy-dandy 9mm-like         บ
 บ  rubber-band pistol.  I think it was a Smith & Wesson, I could be wrong.   บ
 บ  I had my trusty 6 shooter with 1 band left.  Tara (the "girl") was        บ
 บ  sitting on the bed next to me, and I was more or less protecting her      บ
 บ  from Mr. Bitching's savage onslaught.  Later on, about 30 minutes after   บ
 บ  the beginning of the assault, I looked over to see what exactly she was   บ
 บ  doing, and noticed (finally) that her head was on my shoulder and that    บ
 บ  she had her hand on my leg.  Well, this led me to a few interesting       บ
 บ  thoughts, especially as another rubber band slammed into the side of my   บ
 บ  head.  I decided, "Well, shit, this isn't so bad," and let her continue.  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So, another 15 or so minutes pass and we're holding hands, under the  บ
 บ  blanket of infinite protection, with rubber bands sailing all around and  บ
 บ  shit like that.  In general, a very interesting scene, if you can depict  บ
 บ  it.  Well, finally we broke up the battle and her and I just stayed in    บ
 บ  our current positions as Mr. Bitching went off to do something more       บ
 บ  productive.  I think he was in the bathroom, I could be wrong though.     บ
 บ  Old Lefty likes being in the strangest of places, I've heard.  Well, all  บ
 บ  this junk went on for a while, we were mostly just talking and I was      บ
 บ  trying to finger out what exactly this was leading up to.  The thoughts   บ
 บ  in my mind were, needless to say, very nice.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The next day, I went to Tara's grandmother's house to continue        บ
 บ  working on a sprinkler-system we were installing for them.  A bit after   บ
 บ  everybody else was concentrating on the work and everything, I went into  บ
 บ  talk to her.  After the work was finished, we went and got Braveheart,    บ
 บ  and Tara was officially dubbed "my pillow" for the entire movie.  Well,   บ
 บ  that was all fun but not fun enough.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Unfortunately, now that you're getting all riled up and ready for     บ
 บ  some action, nothing more happens here.  I hope this pisses you off,      บ
 บ  because it pissed me off too.  So there.  The statement of hers and Mr.   บ
 บ  Bitching's finally sunk in.  Tara lives in Bakersfield, California.       บ
 บ  Well, that's just a happy ending to my story, ain't it?  So I broke up    บ
 บ  with her, not wanting to hurt her or anything, and I guess I pissed her   บ
 บ  off more than I had wanted to, because now she won't talk to me at all.   บ
 บ  Well, to hell with her.  Ok, finally I've at least cooled down enough to  บ
 บ  continue living, that's my adventure for the day.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      And the moral of this story is - don't start a relationship with      บ
 บ  somebody who lives 1000 miles away.  The End.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Note : This story is 100% true.  The names have not been changed to       บ
 บ         protect the innocent, help your lawn grow, and especially not to   บ
 บ         further the health of the human race.  I hope more people turn     บ
 บ         into chickens or elves in the near future.  Please submit your     บ
 บ         stories.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  ณ   Cracked By: N/A               ณ     Release Date: July 30, 1996       บ
 บ  ณ  Supplied By: The Comet         ณ  Protection Type: None                บ
 บ  ณ  Stripped By: The Comet         ณ        Game Type: Duke Nukem Tools    บ
 บ  ณ  Packaged By: Shadow Master     ณ      Game Rating: 60%                 บ
 บ  รฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤมฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤ  บ
 บ  ณ Requirements: Pentium, 16 MEGS RAM, DOS/WIN95, 163 MEGS HD              บ
 บ  รฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤ  บ
 บ  ณ                                                                         บ
 บ  ณ This is Sierra's first entry into the world of expansions.  This is a   บ
 บ  ณ complete set of tools for Duke Nukem 3D.  Includes features such as     บ
 บ  ณ alien and level design, sound and animation creators, etc.  All new     บ
 บ  ณ single and multi player missions included as well.  Make use of Sierra  บ
 บ  ณ art to do your world designing.  This certainly looks up to typical     บ
 บ  ณ Sierra standards.  We ripped out some included sounds, but it lets you  บ
 บ  ณ make your own.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The content of the above release are available without charge over    บ
 บ  the Internet as well as over other online services.  Sierra On-Line has   บ
 บ  no affiliation with the authors of Duke Nukem 3D, their licensees, or     บ
 บ  the authors of these freely available levels.  Sierra On-Line was merely  บ
 บ  the packager of these free products.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Furthermore, this budget CD sells for $9.99 at your local computer    บ
 บ  software store such as Egghead.  How do I know?  I work at one.           บ
 บ  Basically, Sierra released a lameass freeware CD to make a quick buck,    บ
 บ  and Prestige decided to release the same lameass freeware CD in 48 disks  บ
 บ  so that all the dumbasses out there who decide to waste 48 disks worth    บ
 บ  of download time can get really pissed off at Prestige for pulling off    บ
 บ  this crap.  What I don't understand is that Prestige even goes so far as  บ
 บ  to rate their release a low 60%?  As far as I'm concerned, getting a 60%  บ
 บ  is pretty bad.  When I get 60% on a test, that usually means that I       บ
 บ  fucking flunked.  If Prestige knew that this release was a fucking        บ
 บ  flunk, then why the hell release this crap?                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I also found it interesting that the nfo states, "This certainly      บ
 บ  looks up to typical Sierra standards."  Wow, if that were true, then      บ
 บ  Sierra must have real low standards huh?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, let's look at it on the bright side, at least this freeware     บ
 บ  release is uh... fully cracked.  Keep up the good work.                   บ
