 บ  ฒณ                                                                        บ
 บ  ฒณ Another megahit from Reflux, this time it's 3D scroller beat'em-up     บ
 บ  ฒณ with georgeous gfx and state of the art sfx. It's made by Adeline,     บ
 บ  ฒณ creators of Little Big Adventure, and it's distributed by EA in        บ
 บ  ฒณ Europe and Activision in USA. If you want to know more, and see        บ
 บ  ฒณ things you only dreamt of, go WWW.ACTIVISION.COM and check Time        บ
 บ  ฒณ Commando page. It will blow your mind.                                 บ
 บ  ฒณ                                                                        บ
 บ  ฒณ What was ripped? Levels 02-07 (00, 01, 08 and 09 are 100% full) are    บ
 บ  ฒณ just a short fights instead of long ones. Sorry, there is no way       บ
 บ  ฒณ to fix it. If the public demands it, we will release levels add-on.    บ
 บ  ฒณ Just let us know. Meanwhile, remember to leech ANIMATIONS add-on,      บ
 บ  ฒณ if you need a fancy stuff...                                           บ
 บ  ฒณ                                                                        บ
 บ  ฒณ                                                     JdA/RLX            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      What was ripped from yet another megahit Reflux release?  Oh, just 6  บ
 บ  out of the possible 10 levels of this awesome game.  Why don't you guys   บ
 บ  try to release at least HALF of the game?  You know, there are things     บ
 บ  called demos that companies give out for free.  A demo of Time Commando   บ
 บ  can be found on WWW.ACTIVISION.COM., neato hey?  Demos usually include a  บ
 บ  few levels of the complete game, but you already knew that right?         บ
 บ  Anyway, if the FBI caught me pirating this game, they probably wouldn't   บ
 บ  be able to charge me with much more than pirating a demo, and last time   บ
 บ  I checked, pirating demos are legal.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hey, why don't you guys release the first level of Myst?  I heard     บ
 บ  that Myst is a real good game.  The first level should be oh... about 40  บ
 บ  disks, but heck, it's a release, and it'll live up to Reflux's            บ
 บ  reputation for quality.  Good job Reflux!  Keep up the good work!         บ

 บ    Subject : Things I Learned from Video Games                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TOP 10 LIST!                                                              บ
 บ  ------------                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      10.) There is no problem that cannot be overcome by violence.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      9.)  If you see food lying on the ground, eat it.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      8.)  Smashing things is good.  Many nice things are hidden inside     บ
 บ           other things.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      7.)  If someone dies, they disappear.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      6.)  Money is frequently found lying on the streets.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      5.)  All shopkeepers carry high-tech weaponry.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      4.)  Ninjas are common, and fight in public frequently.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3.)  All martial arts women wear revealing clothes and have great     บ
 บ           bodies.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.)  Gang members frequently all look the same, and often have the    บ
 บ           same names.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  And the number 1 fact learned is :                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.)  200 to 1 odds against you?  NOT a problem.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ    Author  : Genocide                                                      บ
 บ    Subject : You Might Be a Lamer If                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TOP 10 LIST!                                                              บ
 บ  ------------                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      10.) You trade porn in warez channels.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      9.)  You can't get on 2 node public domain boards.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      8.)  The fastest board you are on is a post for credits board.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      7.)  You camp out in channel #TRSI waiting for the group to get back  บ
 บ           from "vacation."                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      6.)  Your ISP = compuserve.com, gnn.com, aol.com, msn.com, or         บ
 บ           prodigy.com.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      5.)  You pay $20 a month to a sysop to leech from his board.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      4.)  You still own an Apple ][Gs, in fact, it's your fastest          บ
 บ           machine.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3.)  You hang out in channel #FATEfiles.  Ummm... i'ts dead, get      บ
 บ           over it.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.)  You hang out at Walmart waiting for new releases.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ      RCN is proud to present to the scene the official RCN t-shirt.  We    บ
 บ  tried to keep the price as low as we could so that everyone can enjoy     บ
 บ  these goodies.  Keeping with RCN's volunteerish spirit to help the scene, บ
 บ  Road Rebel has decided to take it upon himself to make the RCN t-shirts   บ
 บ  available to the masses.  This is a non-profit venture and we hope that   บ
 บ  in many ways, RCN continues to benefit the scene.. even when we are not   บ
 บ  near our computers.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       The RCN logo is approximately 8"x6" printed on the back of a        บ
 บ        HEAVY-duty Fruit of the Loom white t-shirt, the front is plain.     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       A preview of the shirt can viewed upon pressing escape.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Special orders take up to 4 weeks for shipping.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Summary :                                                                 บ
 บ  ---------                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  1.) All RCN issues must be online and available for FREE download.  The   บ
 บ      current issue and back issues must be located in separate file        บ
 บ      directories.  The FULL file_id.diz for the current issue must be      บ
 บ      shown.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  2.) A "Reality Check Network" conference must be set up.  The "rcn        บ
 บ      affiliate board" ansi must be shown somewhere in the login process    บ
 บ      or somewhere in the conference join.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  3.) Sysops must notify all bulletin board users, via nonconference        บ
 บ      specific mass email, of the new issues available for free download.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The new update to the Reality Check Network World Wide Web Site,      บ
 บ  http://www.rcn.org/, adds many new features :                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Speed Optimization : RCN.org is now speed optimized, which means    บ
 บ        you spend less time waiting and more time browsing.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Better Back Issue Access : It's now quick and easy to scan through  บ
 บ        RCN's back issues, each one has its full description online, to     บ
 บ        make searching for the desired issue that much easier.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Better Interface : v2.0 brings an end to the confusing              บ
 บ        conglomeration of pages that previously had existed.  Now speed     บ
 บ        through the icon driven interface to scan back issues of RCN and    บ
 บ        other emags, send comments, read credits, and check out             บ
 บ        merchandise and free files.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Text or JAVA Version : Whatever browser you use can now access the  บ
 บ        RCN.org pages.  Before only Netscape was allowed, but now LYNX and  บ
 บ        other text base users can now access the pages.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       New Look Graphics : The new graphics style are a nice change of     บ
 บ        pace from the hard-edged style of before.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      To become a file mirror, contact us in #RCN on IRC, you must be able  บ
 บ  to store all back issues in a publically accessible directory from the    บ
 บ  WWW.  A link will be created from RCN.org to your site, so users can      บ
 บ  acquire issues from there if the main site becomes overloaded.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RCN WWW Site       : http://www.rcn.org/                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RCN Mirror Site #1 : http://www.halcyon.com/sbecker                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
